                        xpath: "//span[contains(text(), 'Queue')]/following::kat-table-cell[1]",
                        type: 'xpath'
                    }
                ];

                for (const selector of queueSelectors) {
                    let element;
                    if (selector.type === 'xpath') {
                        const result = document.evaluate(
                            selector.xpath,
                            document,
                            null,
                            XPathResult.FIRST_ORDERED_NODE_TYPE,
                            null
                        );
                        element = result.singleNodeValue;
                    } else {
                        element = document.querySelector(selector);
                    }

                    if (element) {
                        return element.textContent.trim();
                    }
                }

                return 'Unknown Queue';
            } catch (error) {
                console.error('Error finding queue:', error);
                return 'Unknown Queue';
            }
        },

        getCaseOwner() {
            try {
                const ownerSpan = document.evaluate(
                    "//span[contains(text(), 'Owner')]/following::kat-table-cell[1]",
                    document,
                    null,
                    XPathResult.FIRST_ORDERED_NODE_TYPE,
                    null
                ).singleNodeValue;

                if (ownerSpan) {
                    return ownerSpan.textContent.trim();
                }

                return null;
            } catch (error) {
                console.error('Error getting case owner:', error);
                return null;
            }
        },

        calculateAHT(type, queue, reasonCode, status) {
            try {
                let aht = 0;
                if (type === 'Paragon') {
                    if (AHT_CONFIG.PARAGON.SPECIAL_REASON_CODES.includes(reasonCode)) {
                        aht = AHT_CONFIG.PARAGON.SPECIAL_REASON_CODE_AHT;
                    } else {
                        const queueName = queue.split('@')[0].toLowerCase();
                        for (const queuePattern in AHT_CONFIG.PARAGON.QUEUE_AHT) {
                            if (queueName.includes(queuePattern.toLowerCase())) {
                                // Get base AHT
                                const baseAHT = AHT_CONFIG.PARAGON.QUEUE_AHT[queuePattern];

                                // Get ASIN count and adjust AHT
                                const asinCount = this.getASINCount();
                                aht = this.calculateAdjustedAHT(baseAHT, asinCount);
                                break;
                            }
                        }
                    }
                } else if (type === 'Photon') {
                    // Determine if it's SME or Regular queue
                    const queueType = queue.toLowerCase().includes('sme') ? 'SME' : 'REGULAR';
                    console.log('Calculating Photon AHT:', {
                        status: status,
                        queueType: queueType
                    });

                    // Clean up status text
                    const cleanStatus = status.replace(/Status|:.*$/g, '').trim();

                    // Try exact match first
                    if (AHT_CONFIG.PHOTON[queueType][cleanStatus]) {
                        aht = AHT_CONFIG.PHOTON[queueType][cleanStatus];
                    } else {
                        // Try partial match if exact match fails
                        for (const [configStatus, configAHT] of Object.entries(AHT_CONFIG.PHOTON[queueType])) {
                            if (cleanStatus.includes(configStatus)) {
                                aht = configAHT;
                                break;
                            }
                        }
                    }

                    console.log('Calculated AHT:', {
                        cleanStatus: cleanStatus,
                        aht: aht,
                        queueType: queueType
                    });
                }

                return aht || 0;
            } catch (error) {
                console.error('Error calculating AHT:', error);
                return 0;
            }
        },
        // Add a debug method for AHT calculation
        debugAHTCalculation(caseData) {
            console.log('AHT Calculation Debug:', {
                caseId: caseData.id,
                type: caseData.type,
                status: caseData.status,
                queue: caseData.queue,
                calculatedAHT: this.calculateAHT(
                    caseData.type,
                    caseData.queue,
                    caseData.reasonCode,
                    caseData.status
                )
            });
        },

        showNotification(caseData) {
            // Check if we've shown this case notification recently
            const caseKey = `${caseData.id}-${caseData.status}`;
            const now = Date.now();

            // If we've shown this exact notification in the last 5 seconds, skip it
            if (this.recentNotifications?.[caseKey] &&
                (now - this.recentNotifications[caseKey]) < 5000) {
                return;
            }

            // Store this notification timestamp
            this.recentNotifications = this.recentNotifications || {};
            this.recentNotifications[caseKey] = now;

            // Remove any existing notifications
            const existingNotifications = document.querySelectorAll('.case-notification');
            existingNotifications.forEach(notification => notification.remove());

            const notification = document.createElement('div');
            notification.className = 'case-notification';
            notification.innerHTML = `
    <div>ID: ${caseData.id}</div>
    <div>Status: ${caseData.status}</div>
`;

            // Add styles if not already present
            if (!document.querySelector('#case-notification-styles')) {
                const styleEl = document.createElement('style');
                styleEl.id = 'case-notification-styles';
                styleEl.textContent = `
        .case-notification {
            position: fixed;
            top: 20px;
            left: 50%;
            transform: translateX(-50%);
            background: #002d5b;
            color: white;
            padding: 12px 20px;
            border-radius: 4px;
            z-index: 10000;
            font-size: 14px;
            box-shadow: 0 2px 8px rgba(0,0,0,0.2);
            opacity: 0;
            transition: opacity 0.3s ease;
        }

        .case-notification.visible {
            opacity: 1;
        }
    `;
                document.head.appendChild(styleEl);
            }

            document.body.appendChild(notification);

            // Trigger reflow and show notification
            notification.offsetHeight;
            requestAnimationFrame(() => {
                notification.classList.add('visible');
            });

            // Remove after delay
            setTimeout(() => {
                notification.classList.remove('visible');
                setTimeout(() => {
                    if (notification && notification.parentElement) {
                        notification.remove();
                    }
                }, 300);
            }, 3000);
        },
        trackAuxChange(status) {
            const today = new Date().toLocaleDateString();
            let auxData = JSON.parse(GM_getValue(`auxData_${today}`) || '{}');

            if (status.toLowerCase() === 'available' || status.toLowerCase() === 'email') {
                if (!auxData.firstAvailable) {
                    auxData.firstAvailable = new Date().toISOString();
                }
            } else if (status.toLowerCase() === 'offline') {
                auxData.lastOffline = new Date().toISOString();
            }

            GM_setValue(`auxData_${today}`, JSON.stringify(auxData));
        },

        updateAUXDisplay(CaseSystem, doc) {
            try {
                // Update AUX Status Badge
                const auxBadge = doc.querySelector('.aux-badge');
                const statusText = doc.querySelector('.aux-status-text');
                const statusDot = doc.querySelector('.aux-status-dot');
                const auxStatusCard = doc.querySelector('.aux-status-card');

                if (auxBadge && statusText && statusDot && auxStatusCard) {
                    const currentStatus = CaseSystem.auxState.currentStatus;
                    statusText.textContent = currentStatus;

                    // Update status colors
                    const statusColors = {
                        'available': '#4caf50',
                        'email': '#2196f3',
                        'break': '#ff9800',
                        'lunch': '#ff9800',
                        'meeting': '#9c27b0',
                        'offline': '#f44336',
                        'training': '#009688'
                    };

                    const color = statusColors[currentStatus.toLowerCase()] || '#757575';
                    auxStatusCard.setAttribute('data-status', currentStatus.toLowerCase());
                    statusDot.style.backgroundColor = color;

                    // Add timestamps section if it doesn't exist
                    if (!doc.querySelector('.aux-timestamps')) {
                        const timestampsDiv = doc.createElement('div');
                        timestampsDiv.className = 'aux-timestamps';
                        timestampsDiv.innerHTML = `
                    <div class="timestamp-row">
                        <span class="timestamp-label">Started at:</span>
                        <span class="timestamp-value" id="startTime">--:--</span>
                    </div>
                    <div class="timestamp-row">
                        <span class="timestamp-label">Last Offline:</span>
                        <span class="timestamp-value" id="lastOffline">--:--</span>
                    </div>
                `;
                        auxStatusCard.appendChild(timestampsDiv);
                    }
                }

                // Update Timer Display
                const [hours, minutes, seconds] = CaseSystem.auxState.duration.split(':');
                const timeValues = doc.querySelectorAll('.time-circle .time-value');

                if (timeValues.length >= 3) {
                    timeValues[0].textContent = hours.padStart(2, '0');
                    timeValues[1].textContent = minutes.padStart(2, '0');
                    timeValues[2].textContent = seconds.padStart(2, '0');

                    // Add animation class for time change
                    timeValues.forEach(value => {
                        value.classList.add('time-update');
                        setTimeout(() => value.classList.remove('time-update'), 300);
                    });
                }

                // Calculate current productive time including active duration
                const currentCategory = CaseSystem.getAuxCategory(CaseSystem.auxState.currentStatus);
                const currentSeconds = this.parseTime(CaseSystem.auxState.duration);

                let totalProductiveSeconds = CaseSystem.auxTotals.dailyTotals.productive;
                if (currentCategory === 'productive') {
                    totalProductiveSeconds += currentSeconds;
                }

                // Calculate start time
                const now = new Date();
                const startTime = new Date(now.getTime() - (totalProductiveSeconds * 1000));

                // Update timestamps display
                const lastOfflineElement = doc.getElementById('lastOffline');
                const startTimeElement = doc.getElementById('startTime');
                if (startTimeElement) {
                    const currentTime = new Date();
                    const productiveSeconds = CaseSystem.auxTotals.dailyTotals.productive +
                          (CaseSystem.getAuxCategory(CaseSystem.auxState.currentStatus) === 'productive' ?
                           CaseSystem.auxTotals.productive : 0);

                    // Calculate start time by subtracting productive time from current time
                    const startTime = new Date(currentTime - (productiveSeconds * 1000));

                    // Format and display the calculated start time
                    startTimeElement.textContent = startTime.toLocaleTimeString('en-US', {
                        hour: '2-digit',
                        minute: '2-digit',
                        hour12: true
                    });
                }

                if (lastOfflineElement) {
                    if (currentStatus.toLowerCase() === 'offline') {
                        lastOfflineElement.textContent = now.toLocaleTimeString('en-US', {
                            hour: '2-digit',
                            minute: '2-digit',
                            hour12: true
                        });
                        lastOfflineElement.classList.remove('active');
                    } else {
                        lastOfflineElement.textContent = 'Currently Active';
                        lastOfflineElement.classList.add('active');
                    }
                }

                // Update Summary Items with Progress Bars
                const totals = {
                    productive: totalProductiveSeconds,
                    nonProductive: CaseSystem.auxTotals.dailyTotals.nonProductive +
                    (currentCategory === 'nonProductive' ? currentSeconds : 0),
                    offline: CaseSystem.auxTotals.dailyTotals.offline +
                    (currentCategory === 'offline' ? currentSeconds : 0)
                };

                // Update summary display
                Object.entries(totals).forEach(([key, seconds]) => {
                    const valueElement = doc.querySelector(`.summary-value.${key}`);
                    if (valueElement) {
                        const hours = Math.floor(seconds / 3600);
                        const minutes = Math.floor((seconds % 3600) / 60);
                        valueElement.textContent = `${hours}h ${minutes}m`;
                    }
                });

                // Calculate and update progress bars
                const totalTime = Object.values(totals).reduce((a, b) => a + b, 0);
                if (totalTime > 0) {
                    Object.entries(totals).forEach(([key, seconds]) => {
                        const progressBar = doc.querySelector(`.progress.${key}`);
                        if (progressBar) {
                            const percentage = (seconds / totalTime) * 100;
                            progressBar.style.width = `${percentage}%`;
                        }
                    });
                }

                console.log('Updated Display Totals:', {
                    currentTime: now.toLocaleTimeString(),
                    totalProductiveSeconds,
                    calculatedStartTime: startTime.toLocaleTimeString(),
                    currentStatus,
                    currentDuration: CaseSystem.auxState.duration,
                    totals
                });

            } catch (error) {
                console.error('Error updating AUX display:', error);
            }
        },

        resetDailyTotals() {
            const today = new Date().toDateString();
            const lastReset = GM_getValue('lastAuxReset');

            if (lastReset !== today) {
                console.log('Performing daily AUX reset');

                // Save previous totals for debugging
                const previousTotals = {...this.auxTotals};

                this.auxTotals = {
                    productive: 0,
                    nonProductive: 0,
                    offline: 0,
                    dailyTotals: {
                        productive: 0,
                        nonProductive: 0,
                        offline: 0
                    },
                    lastStatus: this.auxTotals.lastStatus,
                    lastStatusTime: new Date().toISOString(),
                    isInitialized: true
                };

                GM_setValue('auxTotals', JSON.stringify(this.auxTotals));
                GM_setValue('lastAuxReset', today);

                console.log('Daily reset completed:', {
                    previous: previousTotals,
                    new: this.auxTotals
                });
            }
        },


        getStatusColor(state) {
            const colors = {
                'available': '#4caf50',
                'break': '#ff9800',
                'break2': '#ff9800',
                'break3': '#ff9800',
                'lunch': '#ff9800',
                'meeting': '#purple',
                'email': '#2196f3',
                'offline': '#f44336',
                'personal': '#ff9800',
                'project': '#9c27b0',
                'system': '#607d8b',
                'training': '#009688'
            };
            return colors[state.toLowerCase()] || '#757575';
        },

        updateDashboard() {
            if (window.dashboardWindow && !window.dashboardWindow.closed) {
                // Update timestamp
                const now = new Date();
                const timeString = now.toLocaleTimeString();
                window.dashboardWindow.document.getElementById('lastUpdateTime').textContent = timeString;

                // Update data
                window.dashboardWindow.refreshDashboard();
                window.dashboardWindow.updateCaseManagement();
                window.dashboardWindow.updateDashboardMetrics();
                this.updateAuxDisplay();
            }
        }
    };
    const AHTTracker = {
        targetMinutes: 480,
        milestones: [25, 50, 75, 100],
        lastMilestoneReached: 0,

        showNotification(message, isAchievement = false) {
            const existingPopup = document.querySelector('.target-popup');
            if (existingPopup) existingPopup.remove();

            const popup = document.createElement('div');
            popup.className = 'target-popup';
            popup.innerHTML = message;

            if (isAchievement) {
                popup.style.background = 'linear-gradient(45deg, #4caf50, #45b649)';
            }

            document.body.appendChild(popup);
            setTimeout(() => popup.classList.add('show'), 100);
            setTimeout(() => {
                popup.classList.remove('show');
                setTimeout(() => popup.remove(), 300);
            }, 5000);
        },

        updateAHTDisplay(currentAHT) {
            if (!window.dashboardWindow || window.dashboardWindow.closed) return;

            const doc = window.dashboardWindow.document;
            const ahtElement = doc.getElementById('todayAHT');
            const statusElement = doc.getElementById('ahtStatus');
            const progressBar = doc.getElementById('ahtProgress');

            if (!ahtElement || !statusElement || !progressBar) return;

            // Update AHT display
            ahtElement.textContent = `${currentAHT.toFixed(1)}/${this.targetMinutes} mins`;

            // Calculate percentage
            const percentage = (currentAHT / this.targetMinutes) * 100;
            progressBar.style.width = `${Math.min(100, percentage)}%`;

            // Update status indicator
            if (currentAHT >= this.targetMinutes) {
                statusElement.textContent = '🎯';
                statusElement.title = 'Target Achieved!';
                ahtElement.classList.add('achievement-animation');
                this.showNotification(
                    `<span style="font-size: 20px">🎉</span> Congratulations! You've achieved your daily AHT target!`,
                    true
                );
            } else {
                statusElement.textContent = '⏳';
                statusElement.title = 'Target in Progress';

                // Check for milestones
                const currentMilestone = this.milestones.find(m =>
                                                              percentage >= m && m > this.lastMilestoneReached
                                                             );

                if (currentMilestone) {
                    this.lastMilestoneReached = currentMilestone;
                    this.showNotification(
                        `<span style="font-size: 16px">🎯</span> You've reached ${currentMilestone}% of your daily target!`
                    );
                }

                // Show remaining time every hour or on specific triggers
                const remainingMinutes = this.targetMinutes - currentAHT;
                if (remainingMinutes > 0 && remainingMinutes % 60 === 0) {
                    this.showNotification(
                        `⏳ ${remainingMinutes} minutes remaining to reach your daily target`
                    );
                }
            }
        }
    };
    const PerformanceSummary = {
        currentPeriod: 'weekly',
        charts: {},

        initialize() {
            this.initializeCharts();
            this.updateSummary();

            // Refresh every minute
            setInterval(() => this.updateSummary(), 60000);

            // Set up period selector
            const periodBtns = window.dashboardWindow.document.querySelectorAll('.period-btn');
            periodBtns.forEach(btn => {
                btn.addEventListener('click', () => {
                    periodBtns.forEach(b => b.classList.remove('active'));
                    btn.classList.add('active');
                    this.currentPeriod = btn.dataset.period;
                    this.updateSummary();
                });
            });
        },

        initializeCharts() {
            if (!window.dashboardWindow || window.dashboardWindow.closed) return;

            const doc = window.dashboardWindow.document;
            const dailyCasesCtx = doc.getElementById('dailyCasesTrendChart');
            const efficiencyCtx = doc.getElementById('efficiencyTrendChart');

            if (!dailyCasesCtx || !efficiencyCtx) {
                console.error('Cannot find chart canvas elements');
                return;
            }

            this.charts.dailyCases = new Chart(dailyCasesCtx, {
                type: 'bar',
                data: {
                    labels: [],
                    datasets: [{
                        label: 'Cases',
                        data: [],
                        backgroundColor: '#232f3e'
                    }]
                },
                options: {
                    responsive: true,
                    maintainAspectRatio: false,
                    plugins: {
                        legend: {
                            position: 'right',
                            align: 'center'
                        }
                    }
                }
            });

            this.charts.efficiency = new Chart(efficiencyCtx, {
                type: 'line',
                data: {
                    labels: [],
                    datasets: [{
                        label: 'Efficiency',
                        data: [],
                        borderColor: '#ff9900',
                        tension: 0.4
                    }]
                },
                options: {
                    responsive: true,
                    maintainAspectRatio: false,
                    plugins: {
                        legend: {
                            position: 'right',
                            align: 'center'
                        }
                    }
                }
            });
        },

        calculatePerformanceData() {
            const endDate = new Date();
            const startDate = new Date();
            startDate.setDate(endDate.getDate() - (this.currentPeriod === 'weekly' ? 7 : 30));

            // Get cases within date range
            const periodCases = Object.values(CaseSystem.cases).filter(caseData => {
                const caseDate = new Date(caseData.date);
                return caseDate >= startDate && caseDate <= endDate;
            });

            // Calculate metrics
            const metrics = {
                cases: {
                    total: periodCases.length,
                    paragon: periodCases.filter(c => c.type === 'Paragon').length,
                    photon: periodCases.filter(c => c.type === 'Photon').length,
                    transfers: periodCases.filter(c => c.isTransfer).length
                },
                aht: {
                    paragon: this.calculateAverageAHT(periodCases.filter(c => c.type === 'Paragon')),
                    photon: this.calculateAverageAHT(periodCases.filter(c => c.type === 'Photon')),
                    overall: this.calculateAverageAHT(periodCases)
                },
                auxTime: CaseSystem.auxTotals.dailyTotals,
                efficiency: this.calculateEfficiency(periodCases)
            };

            return metrics;
        },

        updateCharts(data) {
            if (!this.charts.dailyCases || !this.charts.efficiency) return;

            // Update daily cases chart
            const dates = Object.keys(data.dailyCases);
            this.charts.dailyCases.data.labels = dates;
            this.charts.dailyCases.data.datasets[0].data = dates.map(date => data.dailyCases[date].paragon);
            this.charts.dailyCases.data.datasets[1].data = dates.map(date => data.dailyCases[date].photon);
            this.charts.dailyCases.data.datasets[2].data = dates.map(date => data.dailyCases[date].transfers);
            this.charts.dailyCases.update();

            // Update efficiency chart
            this.charts.efficiency.data.labels = dates;
            this.charts.efficiency.data.datasets[0].data = dates.map(date => data.efficiency[date]);
            this.charts.efficiency.update();
        },
        updateSummary() {
            const data = this.calculatePerformanceData();
            const doc = window.dashboardWindow.document;

            // Update Cases Handled
            doc.querySelector('#totalCasesSummary').textContent = data.cases.total;
            doc.querySelector('#paragonCasesSummary').textContent = data.cases.paragon;
            doc.querySelector('#photonCasesSummary').textContent = data.cases.photon;
            doc.querySelector('#transfersCasesSummary').textContent = data.cases.transfers;

            // Update AHT
            doc.querySelector('#avgAHTSummary').textContent =
                `${data.aht.overall.toFixed(1)}`;
            doc.querySelector('#paragonAHTSummary').textContent =
                `${data.aht.paragon.toFixed(1)}`;
            doc.querySelector('#photonAHTSummary').textContent =
                `${data.aht.photon.toFixed(1)}`;

            // Update AUX Time
            doc.querySelector('#productiveTimeSummary').textContent =
                this.formatTime(data.auxTime.productive);
            doc.querySelector('#nonProductiveTimeSummary').textContent =
                this.formatTime(data.auxTime.nonProductive);
            doc.querySelector('#offlineTimeSummary').textContent =
                this.formatTime(data.auxTime.offline);

            // Update Efficiency
            doc.querySelector('#avgEfficiencySummary').textContent =
                `${data.efficiency.toFixed(1)}%`;

            // Update charts
            this.updateCharts(data);
        },

        calculatePerformanceData() {
            const endDate = new Date();
            const startDate = new Date();

            if (this.currentPeriod === 'weekly') {
                startDate.setDate(endDate.getDate() - 7);
            } else {
                startDate.setDate(endDate.getDate() - 30);
            }

            const periodCases = Object.values(CaseSystem.cases).filter(caseData => {
                const caseDate = new Date(caseData.date);
                return caseDate >= startDate && caseDate <= endDate;
            });

            return {
                cases: {
                    total: periodCases.length,
                    paragon: periodCases.filter(c => c.type === 'Paragon').length,
                    photon: periodCases.filter(c => c.type === 'Photon').length,
                    transfers: periodCases.filter(c => c.isTransfer).length
                },
                aht: {
                    paragon: this.calculateAverageAHT(periodCases, 'Paragon'),
                    photon: this.calculateAverageAHT(periodCases, 'Photon'),
                    overall: this.calculateAverageAHT(periodCases)
                },
                efficiency: this.calculateAverageEfficiency(startDate, endDate),
                auxTime: this.calculateAUXDistribution(startDate, endDate)
            };
        },

        calculateAverageAHT(cases, type = null) {
            const filteredCases = type ?
                  cases.filter(c => c.type === type) : cases;

            if (filteredCases.length === 0) return 0;

            const totalAHT = filteredCases.reduce((sum, c) => sum + (c.aht || 0), 0);
            return Math.round((totalAHT / filteredCases.length) * 10) / 10;
        },

        calculateAverageEfficiency(startDate, endDate) {
            return 95.5;
        },

        calculateAUXDistribution(startDate, endDate) {
            return {
                productive: 360,
                nonProductive: 60,
                offline: 30
            };
        },

        updateSummaryCards(data) {
            if (!window.dashboardWindow || window.dashboardWindow.closed) return;

            const doc = window.dashboardWindow.document;

            // Update case counts
            doc.getElementById('totalCasesSummary').textContent = data.cases.total;
            doc.getElementById('paragonCasesSummary').textContent = data.cases.paragon;
            doc.getElementById('photonCasesSummary').textContent = data.cases.photon;
            doc.getElementById('transfersCasesSummary').textContent = data.cases.transfers;

            // Update efficiency
            doc.getElementById('avgEfficiencySummary').textContent =
                `${data.efficiency.toFixed(1)}%`;

            // Update AHT
            doc.getElementById('avgAHTSummary').textContent =
                `${data.aht.overall.toFixed(1)}m`;
            doc.getElementById('paragonAHTSummary').textContent =
                `${data.aht.paragon.toFixed(1)}m`;
            doc.getElementById('photonAHTSummary').textContent =
                `${data.aht.photon.toFixed(1)}m`;

            // Update AUX time
            doc.getElementById('productiveTimeSummary').textContent =
                this.formatTime(data.auxTime.productive);
            doc.getElementById('nonProductiveTimeSummary').textContent =
                this.formatTime(data.auxTime.nonProductive);
            doc.getElementById('offlineTimeSummary').textContent =
                this.formatTime(data.auxTime.offline);
        },

        formatTime(minutes) {
            const hours = Math.floor(minutes / 60);
            const mins = minutes % 60;
            return `${hours}h ${mins}m`;
        }
    };
    CaseSystem.auxEditsInitialized = false;

    async function openDashboard() {
        if (!UserSystem.isLoggedIn()) {
            const username = prompt("Enter your login ID:");
            if (!username) return;
            if (!UserSystem.login(username)) {
                alert("Login failed. Please try again.");
                return;
            }
        }

        // Pre-load data before opening window
        await CaseSystem.processCaseUpdates();
        await CaseSystem.loadStoredAUXData();
        // Initialize AUX edits only if not already initialized
        if (!CaseSystem.auxEditsInitialized) {
            CaseSystem.initializeAUXEdits();
            CaseSystem.auxEditsInitialized = true;
        }

        // Now open the window
        window.dashboardWindow = window.open('', 'AmazonCaseDashboard', 'width=1200,height=800,scrollbars=yes');
        // Check for schedule settings
        if (!GM_getValue('shiftTiming') || !GM_getValue('weekoffPattern')) {
            // Show schedule modal after dashboard loads
            window.dashboardWindow.onload = function() {
                this.editSchedule();
            };
        }

        const allStyles = DASHBOARD_HTML.split('</style>')[0] +
              CASE_MANAGEMENT_STYLES +
              PERFORMANCE_SUMMARY_STYLES +
              '</style>' +
              DASHBOARD_HTML.split('</style>')[1];

        window.dashboardWindow.document.write(allStyles);
        window.dashboardWindow.document.close();

        window.dashboardWindow.Calendar = class Calendar {
            constructor() {
                this.currentDate = new Date();
                this.selectedDate = new Date();
                this.container = this.getContainer();
                this.init();
            }

            getContainer() {
                return window.dashboardWindow.document.querySelector('.calendar-content');
            }

            init() {
                // Set up calendar navigation
                const prevBtn = this.container.querySelector('.prev-month');
                const nextBtn = this.container.querySelector('.next-month');
                const todayBtn = this.container.querySelector('.today-btn');

                prevBtn.addEventListener('click', () => this.previousMonth());
                nextBtn.addEventListener('click', () => this.nextMonth());
                todayBtn.addEventListener('click', () => this.goToToday());

                // Initialize view switchers
                const viewBtns = this.container.querySelectorAll('.view-btn');
                viewBtns.forEach(btn => {
                    btn.addEventListener('click', () => this.switchView(btn.dataset.view));
                });

                // Initial render
                this.renderCalendar();
            }

            renderCalendar() {
                const year = this.currentDate.getFullYear();
                const month = this.currentDate.getMonth();

                // Update header
                const monthYearText = new Date(year, month).toLocaleString('default', {
                    month: 'long',
                    year: 'numeric'
                });
                this.container.querySelector('.current-month').textContent = monthYearText;

                // Calculate days
                const firstDay = new Date(year, month, 1);
                const lastDay = new Date(year, month + 1, 0);
                const daysContainer = this.container.querySelector('.calendar-days');
                daysContainer.innerHTML = '';

                // Previous month's days
                const firstDayIndex = firstDay.getDay();
                for (let i = firstDayIndex; i > 0; i--) {
                    const prevDate = new Date(year, month, -i + 1);
                    this.createDayElement(prevDate, true);
                }

                // Current month's days
                for (let day = 1; day <= lastDay.getDate(); day++) {
                    const date = new Date(year, month, day);
                    this.createDayElement(date);
                }

                // Next month's days
                const lastDayIndex = lastDay.getDay();
                for (let i = 1; i <= 6 - lastDayIndex; i++) {
                    const nextDate = new Date(year, month + 1, i);
                    this.createDayElement(nextDate, true);
                }
            }

            createDayElement(date, isOtherMonth = false) {
                const dayElement = document.createElement('div');
                dayElement.className = 'calendar-day';

                if (isOtherMonth) {
                    dayElement.classList.add('other-month');
                }

                if (this.isToday(date)) {
                    dayElement.classList.add('today');
                }

                // Get metrics for this date
                const metrics = this.getDayMetrics(date);

                // Check for Leave day - when it's a regular day (not weekoff) with no activity
                const isLeave = !metrics.isWeekoff && metrics.cases.total === 0;

                // Add appropriate classes
                if (metrics.isWeekoff) {
                    dayElement.classList.add('weekoff');
                } else if (isLeave) {
                    dayElement.classList.add('leave-day');
                } else {
                    dayElement.classList.add(this.getEfficiencyClass(metrics.efficiency));
                }

                dayElement.innerHTML = `
        <div class="day-header">
            <span class="day-number">${date.getDate()}</span>
            <div class="status-badges">
                ${this.getStatusBadge(metrics, isLeave)}
            </div>
        </div>

        <div class="day-content">
            ${isLeave ? `
                <div class="leave-indicator">
                    <span class="material-icons">event_busy</span>
                    <span>Leave</span>
                </div>
            ` : metrics.cases.total > 0 ? `
                <div class="case-summary">
                    <div class="case-count ${this.getCaseCountClass(metrics.cases.total)}">
                        ${metrics.cases.total} cases
                    </div>
                    <div class="case-breakdown">
                        ${metrics.cases.paragon ? `<div class="paragon">P: ${metrics.cases.paragon}</div>` : ''}
                        ${metrics.cases.photon ? `<div class="photon">Ph: ${metrics.cases.photon}</div>` : ''}
                        ${metrics.cases.transfers ? `<div class="transfer">T: ${metrics.cases.transfers}</div>` : ''}
                    </div>
                </div>
                <div class="metrics-bar">
                    <div class="productive-bar" style="width: ${Math.min((metrics.productive.hours/8) * 100, 100)}%"
                         title="Productive Time: ${metrics.productive.time}">
                    </div>
                </div>
            ` : ''}
        </div>

        <div class="day-tooltip">${this.createTooltipContent(metrics, date, isLeave)}</div>
    `;

                // Add hover listeners for tooltip
                dayElement.addEventListener('mouseenter', () => {
                    const tooltip = dayElement.querySelector('.day-tooltip');
                    tooltip.classList.add('visible');
                });

                dayElement.addEventListener('mouseleave', () => {
                    const tooltip = dayElement.querySelector('.day-tooltip');
                    tooltip.classList.remove('visible');
                });

                this.container.querySelector('.calendar-days').appendChild(dayElement);
            }

            // Update the status badge function
            getStatusBadge(metrics, isLeave) {
                if (metrics.isWeekoff) {
                    return `<span class="badge weekoff-badge">Weekoff</span>`;
                }
                if (isLeave) {
                    return `<span class="badge leave-badge">Leave</span>`;
                }
                if (metrics.cases.total > 0) {
                    return `<span class="badge ${metrics.efficiency >= 100 ? 'high-efficiency' : ''}">
            ${metrics.efficiency}%
        </span>`;
                }
                return '';
            }


            getEfficiencyClass(efficiency) {
                if (efficiency >= 150) return 'efficiency-very-high';
                if (efficiency >= 100) return 'efficiency-high';
                if (efficiency >= 90) return 'efficiency-good';
                return 'efficiency-low';
            }

            getCaseCountClass(count) {
                if (count >= 150) return 'count-very-high';
                if (count >= 120) return 'count-high';
                if (count >= 90) return 'count-medium';
                return 'count-normal';
            }

            createStatusIndicators(metrics) {
                const indicators = [];

                // High ASIN indicator
                if (this.hasHighAsinCases(metrics)) {
                    indicators.push(`
            <span class="status-indicator asin-indicator" title="Has High ASIN Cases">
                <span class="material-icons">format_list_numbered</span>
            </span>
        `);
                }

                // OT indicator
                if (metrics.productive.hours > 9) {
                    indicators.push(`
            <span class="status-indicator ot-indicator" title="Overtime Day">
                <span class="material-icons">schedule</span>
            </span>
        `);
                }

                // High efficiency indicator
                if (metrics.efficiency >= 100) {
                    indicators.push(`
            <span class="status-indicator efficiency-indicator" title="Target Achieved">
                <span class="material-icons">stars</span>
            </span>
        `);
                }

                return indicators.join('');
            }

            createProgressBars(metrics) {
                // Calculate percentages
                const productivePercent = Math.min((metrics.productive.hours / 8) * 100, 100);
                const targetCases = 100; // Set your target
                const casesPercent = Math.min((metrics.cases.total / targetCases) * 100, 100);

                return `
        <div class="progress-bars">
            <div class="progress-bar productive-bar" title="Productive Time: ${metrics.productive.time}">
                <div class="progress" style="width: ${productivePercent}%"></div>
            </div>
            <div class="progress-bar cases-bar" title="Cases: ${metrics.cases.total}">
                <div class="progress" style="width: ${casesPercent}%"></div>
            </div>
        </div>
    `;
            }

            createCaseIndicator(metrics) {
                const total = metrics.cases.total;
                let sizeClass = 'small';

                if (total > 150) sizeClass = 'xlarge';
                else if (total > 120) sizeClass = 'large';
                else if (total > 90) sizeClass = 'medium';

                return `
        <div class="case-indicator ${sizeClass}">
            <span class="case-count">${total}</span>
            <div class="case-breakdown">
                <span class="paragon" style="width: ${(metrics.cases.paragon/total)*100}%"></span>
                <span class="photon" style="width: ${(metrics.cases.photon/total)*100}%"></span>
                <span class="transfer" style="width: ${(metrics.cases.transfers/total)*100}%"></span>
            </div>
        </div>
    `;
            }

            createMetricsDisplay(metrics) {
                return `
        <div class="metrics-display">
            <span class="efficiency ${this.getEfficiencyClass(metrics.efficiency)}">
                ${metrics.efficiency}%
            </span>
            <span class="productive-time">
                ${metrics.productive.hours}h
            </span>
        </div>
    `;
            }

            getDayStatus(metrics, isWeekoff) {
                if (isWeekoff) {
                    return {
                        type: 'weekoff',
                        label: 'Weekoff',
                        class: 'weekoff'
                    };
                }

                // Check for Leave - when it's a regular day with no productive time and no cases
                if (metrics.productive.totalMinutes === 0 && metrics.cases.total === 0) {
                    return {
                        type: 'leave',
                        label: 'Leave',
                        class: 'leave'
                    };
                }

                return {
                    type: 'regular',
                    label: 'Regular Day',
                    class: 'regular-day'
                };
            }

            getDayMetrics(date) {
                const dateStr = date.toDateString();
                const localeDateStr = date.toLocaleDateString();
                const cases = Object.values(CaseSystem.cases).filter(caseData =>
                                                                     new Date(caseData.date).toDateString() === dateStr
                                                                    );

                // Get AUX data matching Analytics calculation
                let productiveSeconds = 0;
                const storedAuxData = GM_getValue(`auxData_${localeDateStr}`);

                if (localeDateStr === new Date().toLocaleDateString()) {
                    // For today - include current status
                    productiveSeconds = CaseSystem.auxTotals.dailyTotals.productive +
                        (CaseSystem.getAuxCategory(CaseSystem.auxState.currentStatus) === 'productive' ?
                         CaseSystem.auxTotals.productive : 0);
                } else if (storedAuxData) {
                    // For historical dates
                    const auxData = typeof storedAuxData === 'string' ?
                          JSON.parse(storedAuxData) : storedAuxData;
                    productiveSeconds = auxData.productive || 0;
                }

                // Calculate AHT with ASIN adjustments
                const ahtDetails = cases.reduce((acc, caseData) => {
                    let baseAHT = parseFloat(caseData.aht) || 0;
                    let asinAdjustment = 0;

                    if (caseData.asinCount > 3) {
                        asinAdjustment = ((caseData.asinCount - 3) * 30) / 60;
                        baseAHT += asinAdjustment;
                    }

                    if (caseData.type === 'Paragon') {
                        acc.paragonAHT += baseAHT;
                    } else if (caseData.type === 'Photon') {
                        acc.photonAHT += baseAHT;
                    } else if (caseData.isTransfer) {
                        acc.transferAHT += 1.5; // Standard transfer AHT
                    }

                    acc.totalAHT += baseAHT;
                    acc.totalAsinAdjustment += asinAdjustment;
                    return acc;
                }, {
                    totalAHT: 0,
                    paragonAHT: 0,
                    photonAHT: 0,
                    transferAHT: 0,
                    totalAsinAdjustment: 0
                });

                // Calculate productive time and efficiency
                const productiveMinutes = Math.max(Math.floor(productiveSeconds / 60), 1);
                const efficiency = CaseSystem.calculateEfficiency(
                    ahtDetails.totalAHT,
                    productiveMinutes
                );

                // Format productive time
                const productiveHours = Math.floor(productiveSeconds / 3600);
                const productiveMinutesRemainder = Math.floor((productiveSeconds % 3600) / 60);

                return {
                    cases: {
                        total: cases.length,
                        paragon: cases.filter(c => c.type === 'Paragon').length,
                        photon: cases.filter(c => c.type === 'Photon').length,
                        transfers: cases.filter(c => c.isTransfer).length
                    },
                    productive: {
                        time: `${productiveHours}h ${productiveMinutesRemainder}m`,
                        hours: productiveHours,
                        minutes: productiveMinutesRemainder,
                        totalMinutes: productiveMinutes
                    },
                    aht: {
                        total: ahtDetails.totalAHT.toFixed(1),
                        paragon: ahtDetails.paragonAHT.toFixed(1),
                        photon: ahtDetails.photonAHT.toFixed(1),
                        transfer: ahtDetails.transferAHT.toFixed(1),
                        asinAdjustment: ahtDetails.totalAsinAdjustment.toFixed(1)
                    },
                    efficiency: efficiency,
                    isWeekoff: this.isWeekoff(date)
                };
            }


            createTooltipContent(metrics, date) {
                return `
        <div class="tooltip-content">
            <div class="tooltip-header">
                ${date.toLocaleDateString('en-US', {
                    weekday: 'long',
                    month: 'long',
                    day: 'numeric'
                })}
                <span class="day-type ${metrics.isWeekoff ? 'weekoff' : 'regular-day'}">
                    ${metrics.isWeekoff ? 'Weekoff' : 'Regular Day'}
                </span>
            </div>

            <div class="tooltip-section">
                <h4>Cases (${metrics.cases.total})</h4>
                <div class="breakdown">
                    <div class="metric-row">
                        <span class="label">Paragon:</span>
                        <span class="value">${metrics.cases.paragon}</span>
                    </div>
                    <div class="metric-row">
                        <span class="label">Photon:</span>
                        <span class="value">${metrics.cases.photon}</span>
                    </div>
                    <div class="metric-row">
                        <span class="label">Transfers:</span>
                        <span class="value">${metrics.cases.transfers}</span>
                    </div>
                </div>
            </div>

            <div class="tooltip-section">
                <h4>Time & Efficiency</h4>
                <div class="breakdown">
                    <div class="metric-row">
                        <span class="label">Productive Time:</span>
                        <span class="value">${metrics.productive.time}</span>
                    </div>
                    <div class="metric-row">
                        <span class="label">Total AHT:</span>
                        <span class="value">${metrics.aht.total}m</span>
                        ${metrics.aht.asinAdjustment > 0 ?
                    `<span class="asin-adjustment">(+${metrics.aht.asinAdjustment}m ASIN)</span>`
                : ''}
                    </div>
                    <div class="metric-row">
                        <span class="label">AHT Breakdown:</span>
                        <div class="aht-breakdown">
                            ${metrics.aht.paragon > 0 ? `<div>P: ${metrics.aht.paragon}m</div>` : ''}
                            ${metrics.aht.photon > 0 ? `<div>Ph: ${metrics.aht.photon}m</div>` : ''}
                            ${metrics.aht.transfer > 0 ? `<div>T: ${metrics.aht.transfer}m</div>` : ''}
                        </div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="metric-row">
                        <span class="label">Efficiency:</span>
                        <span class="value efficiency ${this.getEfficiencyClass(metrics.efficiency)}">
                            ${metrics.efficiency}%
                        </span>
                    </div>
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>
    `;
            }

            getEfficiencyClass(efficiency) {
                if (efficiency >= 150) return 'very-high';
                if (efficiency >= 100) return 'high';
                if (efficiency >= 90) return 'good';
                return 'low';
            }

            isWeekoff(date) {
                // Get weekoff pattern from settings
                const weekoffPattern = GM_getValue('weekoffPattern', 'sunmon');
                const day = date.toLocaleDateString('en-US', { weekday: 'short' }).toLowerCase();

                // Check if the day is in weekoff pattern
                return weekoffPattern.includes(day);
            }

            getCaseDataForDate(date) {
                // Filter cases for this date
                const dateStr = date.toDateString();
                const cases = Object.values(CaseSystem.cases).filter(caseData => {
                    return new Date(caseData.date).toDateString() === dateStr;
                });

                return {
                    total: cases.length,
                    paragon: cases.filter(c => c.type === 'Paragon').length,
                    photon: cases.filter(c => c.type === 'Photon').length,
                    transfers: cases.filter(c => c.isTransfer).length
                };
            }

            generateDayContent(caseData) {
                if (!caseData.total) return '';

                return `
            <div class="day-metrics">
                <div class="case-count">
                    <span class="total">${caseData.total}</span> cases
                </div>
                ${caseData.paragon ? `<div class="paragon">P: ${caseData.paragon}</div>` : ''}
                ${caseData.photon ? `<div class="photon">Ph: ${caseData.photon}</div>` : ''}
                ${caseData.transfers ? `<div class="transfers">T: ${caseData.transfers}</div>` : ''}
            </div>
        `;
            }

            isToday(date) {
                const today = new Date();
                return date.toDateString() === today.toDateString();
            }

            previousMonth() {
                this.currentDate.setMonth(this.currentDate.getMonth() - 1);
                this.renderCalendar();
            }

            nextMonth() {
                this.currentDate.setMonth(this.currentDate.getMonth() + 1);
                this.renderCalendar();
            }

            goToToday() {
                this.currentDate = new Date();
                this.renderCalendar();
            }

            switchView(view) {
                const viewBtns = this.container.querySelectorAll('.view-btn');
                viewBtns.forEach(btn => {
                    btn.classList.toggle('active', btn.dataset.view === view);
                });
                // Implement different view renders here
            }
        };

        window.dashboardWindow.onload = async function() {
            try {
                // Show loading indicator
                const loadingEl = this.document.querySelector('.loading-overlay');
                if (loadingEl) loadingEl.style.display = 'flex';

                // Initialize dashboard immediately with pre-loaded data
                await initializeDashboard();

                // Update all metrics immediately
                this.updateDashboardMetrics();
                this.updateCaseManagement();
                CaseSystem.updateAuxDisplay();
                // Initialize Calendar
                if (!this.calendarInstance && this.document.querySelector('.calendar-content')) {
                    this.calendarInstance = new this.Calendar();
                }

                // Add the analytics date picker initialization here
                if (this.document.getElementById('analyticsDatePicker')) {
                    this.document.getElementById('analyticsDatePicker').addEventListener('change', (e) => {
                        this.updateCharts(e.target.value);
                    });
                }

                // Initialize the AUX timestamps section if it doesn't exist
                const auxCard = this.document.querySelector('.aux-status-card');
                if (auxCard && !auxCard.querySelector('.aux-timestamps')) {
                    const timestampsDiv = document.createElement('div');
                    timestampsDiv.className = 'aux-timestamps';
                    timestampsDiv.innerHTML = `
                <div class="timestamp-row">
                    <span class="timestamp-label">Started at:</span>
                    <span class="timestamp-value" id="startTime">--:--</span>
                </div>
                <div class="timestamp-row">
                    <span class="timestamp-label">Last Offline:</span>
                    <span class="timestamp-value" id="lastOffline">--:--</span>
                </div>
            `;
                    auxCard.appendChild(timestampsDiv);
                }

                // Initial update of timestamps
                this.updateAuxTimestamps();
                // Initialize all components
                this.PerformanceSummary = PerformanceSummary;
                await this.PerformanceSummary.initialize();
                AHTTracker.lastMilestoneReached = 0;
                QuickStats.init();
                QuickStats.update();

                // Initialize charts if needed
                if (this.document.querySelector('.analytics-content')) {
                    this.initializeCharts();
                    this.updateCharts();
                }


                // Hide loading indicator
                if (loadingEl) loadingEl.style.display = 'none';

            } catch (error) {
                console.error('Error initializing dashboard:', error);
                const loadingEl = this.document.querySelector('.loading-overlay');
                if (loadingEl) loadingEl.style.display = 'none';
            }
        };
        window.dashboardWindow.updateAuxTimestamps = function() {
            const startTimeElement = this.document.getElementById('startTime');
            if (startTimeElement) {
                const currentTime = new Date();
                const productiveSeconds = CaseSystem.auxTotals.dailyTotals.productive +
                      (CaseSystem.getAuxCategory(CaseSystem.auxState.currentStatus) === 'productive' ?
                       CaseSystem.auxTotals.productive : 0);

                if (productiveSeconds > 0) {
                    const startTime = new Date(currentTime - (productiveSeconds * 1000));
                    startTimeElement.textContent = startTime.toLocaleTimeString('en-US', {
                        hour: '2-digit',
                        minute: '2-digit',
                        hour12: true
                    });
                }
            }
        };

        // Add styles to dashboard window
        const styleElement = window.dashboardWindow.document.createElement('style');
        styleElement.textContent = PERFORMANCE_SUMMARY_STYLES;
        window.dashboardWindow.document.head.appendChild(styleElement);

        console.log('Export process started');
        console.log('Current cases:', CaseSystem.cases);

            // Add Reset functionality
            document.getElementById('resetAUX').addEventListener('click', () => {
                // Show confirmation dialog
                if (confirm('Are you sure you want to reset all AUX times for today? This cannot be undone.')) {
                    const today = new Date().toLocaleDateString();

                    // Reset all stored values in GM storage
                    let existingData = JSON.parse(GM_getValue(`auxData_${today}`) || '{}');
                    GM_setValue(`auxData_${today}`, JSON.stringify({
                        productive: 0,
                        nonProductive: 0,
                        offline: 0,
                        weekoffPattern: existingData.weekoffPattern || GM_getValue('weekoffPattern', 'sunmon')
                    }));

                    // Reset auxEdits
                    let auxEdits = GM_getValue('auxEdits', {});
                    if (auxEdits[today]) {
                        delete auxEdits[today];
                        GM_setValue('auxEdits', auxEdits);
                    }

                    // Reset auxState
                    GM_setValue('auxState', JSON.stringify({
                        currentStatus: CaseSystem.auxState.currentStatus,
                        duration: '0:00:00',
                        lastCheck: new Date().toISOString()
                    }));

                    // Reset auxTotals
                    GM_setValue('auxTotals', JSON.stringify({
                        productive: 0,
                        nonProductive: 0,
                        offline: 0,
                        dailyTotals: {
                            productive: 0,
                            nonProductive: 0,
                            offline: 0
                        },
                        lastStatus: CaseSystem.auxState.currentStatus,
                        lastStatusTime: new Date().toISOString(),
                        isInitialized: true
                    }));

                    // Reset CaseSystem's current values
                    CaseSystem.auxTotals = {
                        productive: 0,
                        nonProductive: 0,
                        offline: 0,
                        dailyTotals: {
                            productive: 0,
                            nonProductive: 0,
                            offline: 0
                        },
                        lastStatus: CaseSystem.auxState.currentStatus,
                        lastStatusTime: new Date().toISOString(),
                        isInitialized: true
                    };

                    CaseSystem.auxState = {
                        currentStatus: CaseSystem.auxState.currentStatus,
                        duration: '0:00:00',
                        lastCheck: new Date().toISOString()
                    };

                    // Update display
                    this.updateAuxDisplay();

                    // Show success notification
                    const notification = document.createElement('div');
                    notification.className = 'aux-notification';
                    notification.textContent = 'AUX times have been reset for today';
                    notification.style.cssText = `
            position: fixed;
            top: 20px;
            left: 50%;
            transform: translateX(-50%);
            background: #4caf50;
            color: white;
            padding: 12px 24px;
            border-radius: 4px;
            z-index: 10000;
        `;
                    document.body.appendChild(notification);
                    setTimeout(() => notification.remove(), 3000);

                    // Close modal
                    modal.remove();
                }
            });

            // Existing Add Time functionality
            document.getElementById('saveAUX').addEventListener('click', () => {

                modal.remove();
            });

        };

        const OT_THRESHOLDS = {
            REGULAR_MIN: 1,    // Minimum 1 hour for regular day OT
            REGULAR_MAX: 2,    // Maximum 2 hours for regular day OT
            WEEKOFF_MAX: 10    // Maximum 10 hours for weekoff (6th day) OT
