        window.dashboardWindow.calculateOTMetrics = function(selectedMonth = null) {
            // Determine target date based on selection
            let targetDate;
            if (selectedMonth) {
                // Parse selected month (format: "YYYY-MM")
                const [year, month] = selectedMonth.split('-').map(Number);
                targetDate = new Date(year, month - 1); // month is 0-based
            } else {
                targetDate = new Date();
            }

            // Get dates for target month
            const firstDay = new Date(targetDate.getFullYear(), targetDate.getMonth(), 1);
            const lastDay = new Date(targetDate.getFullYear(), targetDate.getMonth() + 1, 0);
            const today = new Date().toLocaleDateString();

            let monthlyOT = {
                total: 0,
                regularDays: 0,
                weekoffDays: 0,
                details: [],
                month: `${targetDate.getFullYear()}-${String(targetDate.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0')}`
            };

            // Get selected schedule
            const weekoffPattern = GM_getValue('weekoffPattern', 'sunmon');

            // Weekoff detection remains same
            const isWeekoff = (date) => {
                const day = date.toLocaleDateString('en-US', { weekday: 'short' }).toLowerCase();
                const weekoffs = weekoffPattern.match(/[a-z]{3}/g);
                const isWeekoffDay = weekoffs.includes(day);
                console.log('Weekoff Check:', {
                    date: date.toLocaleDateString(),
                    day: day,
                    weekoffs: weekoffs,
                    isWeekoffDay: isWeekoffDay
                });
                return isWeekoffDay;
            };

            // Loop through each day of the selected month
            for(let d = new Date(firstDay); d <= lastDay; d.setDate(d.getDate() + 1)) {
                const dateStr = d.toLocaleDateString();
                const isCurrentDay = dateStr === today;

                let totalWorkHours = 0;
                const storedData = GM_getValue(`auxData_${dateStr}`);

                if (storedData || isCurrentDay) {
                    // Calculate work hours
                    if (isCurrentDay && targetDate.getMonth() === new Date().getMonth()) {
                        // Only include current day calculation if we're looking at current month
                        const currentProductiveSeconds = CaseSystem.auxTotals.dailyTotals.productive +
                              (CaseSystem.getAuxCategory(CaseSystem.auxState.currentStatus) === 'productive' ?
                               CaseSystem.auxTotals.productive : 0);
                        totalWorkHours = currentProductiveSeconds / 3600;
                    } else if (storedData) {
                        const auxData = JSON.parse(storedData);
                        totalWorkHours = (auxData.productive || 0) / 3600;
                    }

                    if (totalWorkHours > 0) {
                        const isWeekoffDay = isWeekoff(d);
                        let otHours = 0;

                        if (isWeekoffDay) {
                            otHours = totalWorkHours;
                            monthlyOT.weekoffDays += otHours;

                            console.log('Weekoff OT detected:', {
                                date: dateStr,
                                workHours: totalWorkHours,
                                otHours: otHours
                            });
                        } else if (totalWorkHours > 8) {
                            otHours = Math.min(totalWorkHours - 8, 2);
                            monthlyOT.regularDays += otHours;
                        }

                        if (otHours > 0) {
                            monthlyOT.details.push({
                                date: dateStr,
                                total: otHours,
                                isWeekoff: isWeekoffDay,
                                workHours: totalWorkHours
                            });
                            monthlyOT.total += otHours;
                        }
                    }
                }
            }

            console.log('Monthly OT Calculation:', {
                month: monthlyOT.month,
                total: monthlyOT.total,
                weekoffDays: monthlyOT.weekoffDays,
                regularDays: monthlyOT.regularDays,
                details: monthlyOT.details
            });

            return monthlyOT;
        };

        // Add this helper function to format time
        window.dashboardWindow.formatOTTime = function(hours) {
            const h = Math.floor(hours);
            const m = Math.round((hours - h) * 60);
            return `${h}h ${m}m`;
        };

        // Add this state variable at the top level
        window.dashboardWindow.selectedOTMonth = null;

        // Modify updateOTDisplay
        window.dashboardWindow.updateOTDisplay = function(selectedMonth = null) {
            // If a month is explicitly selected, update the stored state
            if (selectedMonth) {
                this.selectedOTMonth = selectedMonth;
            }

            const availableMonths = this.getAvailableOTMonths();

            // Use stored selection or default to most recent month
            const currentSelection = this.selectedOTMonth || availableMonths[0];

            // Update month selector
            const monthSelect = this.document.getElementById('otMonthSelect');
            if (monthSelect) {
                monthSelect.innerHTML = availableMonths.map(month => {
                    const [year, monthNum] = month.split('-');
                    const monthName = new Date(year, monthNum - 1).toLocaleString('default', { month: 'long' });
                    return `<option value="${month}" ${month === currentSelection ? 'selected' : ''}>
                ${monthName} ${year}
            </option>`;
                }).join('');

                // Add change listener if not already added
                if (!monthSelect.hasListener) {
                    monthSelect.addEventListener('change', (e) => {
                        this.selectedOTMonth = e.target.value; // Update stored state
                        this.updateOTDisplay(e.target.value);
                    });
                    monthSelect.hasListener = true;
                }

                // Ensure dropdown shows correct value
                monthSelect.value = currentSelection;
            }

            // Calculate OT metrics using stored selection
            const otMetrics = this.calculateOTMetrics(currentSelection);

            // Rest of your existing display update code...
            const totalOTDisplay = this.document.getElementById('totalOTHours');
            const regularOTDisplay = this.document.getElementById('regularDayOT');
            const weekoffOTDisplay = this.document.getElementById('weekoffOT');
            const otDetailsDisplay = this.document.getElementById('otDetails');

            if (totalOTDisplay) totalOTDisplay.textContent = this.formatOTTime(otMetrics.total);
            if (regularOTDisplay) regularOTDisplay.textContent = `Regular Days: ${this.formatOTTime(otMetrics.regularDays)}`;
            if (weekoffOTDisplay) weekoffOTDisplay.textContent = `Weekoff Days: ${this.formatOTTime(otMetrics.weekoffDays)}`;

            // Update details section
            if (otDetailsDisplay && otMetrics.details.length > 0) {
                const sortedDetails = otMetrics.details
                .sort((a, b) => new Date(a.date) - new Date(b.date))
                .filter(detail => {
                    if (detail.isWeekoff) return detail.total > 0;
                    return detail.total > 0.5;
                });

                otDetailsDisplay.innerHTML = `
            <div class="ot-details-header">
                ${new Date(otMetrics.month).toLocaleString('default', { month: 'long', year: 'numeric' })} Breakdown
            </div>
            ${sortedDetails.map(detail => `
                <div class="ot-detail-row ${detail.isWeekoff ? 'weekoff' : ''}">
                    <span>${new Date(detail.date).toLocaleDateString()}</span>
                    <span>${detail.isWeekoff ? 'Weekoff' : ''}</span>
                    <span>${this.formatOTTime(detail.total)}</span>
                </div>
            `).join('')}
        `;
            }

            // Log for debugging
            console.log('OT Display Update:', {
                selectedMonth: currentSelection,
                availableMonths: availableMonths,
                metrics: otMetrics
            });
        };

        window.dashboardWindow.getAvailableOTMonths= function() {
            const months = new Set();
            const today = new Date();

            // Look back up to 6 months
            for (let i = 0; i < 6; i++) {
                const date = new Date(today.getFullYear(), today.getMonth() - i, 1);
                const monthKey = `${date.getFullYear()}-${String(date.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0')}`;

                // Check if we have data for this month
                const firstDay = new Date(date.getFullYear(), date.getMonth(), 1);
                const lastDay = new Date(date.getFullYear(), date.getMonth() + 1, 0);

                // Check each day in month for OT data
                for (let d = new Date(firstDay); d <= lastDay; d.setDate(d.getDate() + 1)) {
                    const dateStr = d.toLocaleDateString();
                    const auxData = GM_getValue(`auxData_${dateStr}`);
                    if (auxData) {
                        months.add(monthKey);
                        break;
                    }
                }
            }

            return Array.from(months).sort().reverse(); // Most recent first
        };

        window.dashboardWindow.initializeExportFeatures = function() {
            // Set up export button listener
            const exportBtn = this.document.querySelector('.export-btn');
            if (exportBtn) {
                exportBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
                    console.log('Export button clicked');
                    this.exportCaseData();
                });
            }

            // Add export functionality
            this.exportCaseData = function() {
                try {
                    const cases = CaseSystem.cases;
                    console.log('Starting export with cases:', cases);

                    if (!cases || Object.keys(cases).length === 0) {
                        alert('No data to export');
                        return;
                    }

                    // Get filter values
                    const dateFrom = this.document.getElementById('dateFrom')?.value;
                    const dateTo = this.document.getElementById('dateTo')?.value;
                    const caseType = this.document.getElementById('caseTypeFilter')?.value;
                    const queueFilter = this.document.getElementById('queueFilter')?.value;

                    // Filter cases
                    const filteredCases = Object.values(cases).filter(caseData => {
                        const caseDate = new Date(caseData.date).toISOString().split('T')[0];

                        if (dateFrom && caseDate < dateFrom) return false;
                        if (dateTo && caseDate > dateTo) return false;
                        if (caseType && caseData.type !== caseType &&
                            !(caseData.isTransfer && caseType === 'Transfer')) return false;
                        if (queueFilter && caseData.queue !== queueFilter &&
                            !caseData.isTransfer) return false;

                        return true;
                    });

                    if (filteredCases.length === 0) {
                        alert('No cases match the selected filters');
                        return;
                    }

                    // Create CSV content
                    let csvContent = 'Date,Case ID,Type,Queue,Status,Reason Code,AHT (min)\n';

                    filteredCases
                        .sort((a, b) => new Date(b.date) - new Date(a.date))
                        .forEach(caseData => {
                        const row = [
                            new Date(caseData.date).toLocaleDateString(),
                            caseData.id,
                            caseData.isTransfer ? 'Transfer' : caseData.type,
                            caseData.isTransfer ? 'N/A' : (caseData.queue || 'N/A'),
                            caseData.status || 'N/A',
                            caseData.isTransfer ? 'N/A' : (caseData.reasonCode || 'N/A'),
                            caseData.aht || '0'
                        ];
                        csvContent += row.map(cell =>
                                              `"${String(cell).replace(/"/g, '""')}"`).join(',') + '\n';
                    });

                    // Create and trigger download
                    const blob = new Blob([csvContent], { type: 'text/csv;charset=utf-8;' });
                    const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
                    const downloadLink = document.createElement('a');
                    downloadLink.href = url;
                    downloadLink.download = `case_data_${new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0]}.csv`;

                    // Add to document, click, and cleanup
                    document.body.appendChild(downloadLink);
                    downloadLink.click();
                    document.body.removeChild(downloadLink);
                    URL.revokeObjectURL(url);

                    // Show success notification
                    this.showExportNotification(filteredCases.length);

                } catch (error) {
                    console.error('Export error:', error);
                    alert('Error exporting data: ' + error.message);
                }
            };

            // Add notification helper
            this.showExportNotification = function(count) {
                const notification = document.createElement('div');
                notification.style.cssText = `
            position: fixed;
            top: 20px;
            left: 50%;
            transform: translateX(-50%);
            background: #4caf50;
            color: white;
            padding: 12px 24px;
            border-radius: 4px;
            z-index: 10000;
            font-size: 14px;
            box-shadow: 0 2px 8px rgba(0,0,0,0.2);
        `;
                notification.textContent = `Exported ${count} cases successfully`;
                document.body.appendChild(notification);

                setTimeout(() => notification.remove(), 3000);
            };
        };


        // Add export function directly to window
        window.dashboardWindow.exportCaseData = function() {
            try {
                const doc = window.dashboardWindow.document;

                // Get selected date and filters
                const selectedDateElement = doc.getElementById('selectedDate');
                const selectedDate = selectedDateElement ?
                      selectedDateElement.value || new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0] :
                new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0];
                const caseType = doc.getElementById('caseTypeFilter')?.value;
                const queueFilter = doc.getElementById('queueFilter')?.value;

                // Filter cases
                const filteredCases = Object.values(CaseSystem.cases)
                .filter(caseData => {
                    const caseDate = new Date(caseData.date).toISOString().split('T')[0];

                    // Apply date filter
                    if (caseDate !== selectedDate) return false;

                    // Apply other filters
                    if (caseType && caseData.type !== caseType &&
                        !(caseData.isTransfer && caseType === 'Transfer')) return false;
                    if (queueFilter && caseData.queue !== queueFilter &&
                        !caseData.isTransfer) return false;

                    return true;
                })
                .sort((a, b) => new Date(b.date) - new Date(a.date));

                if (filteredCases.length === 0) {
                    alert('No cases to export for the selected filters');
                    return;
                }

                // Create CSV content with Date instead of Time
                let csvContent = 'Date,Case ID,Type,Queue,Status,Reason Code,AHT (min),ASIN Count,ASIN Adjustment\n';

                filteredCases.forEach(caseData => {
                    const asinAdjustment = caseData.asinCount > 3 ?
                          ((caseData.asinCount - 3) * 30 / 60).toFixed(1) : '0';

                    const caseDate = new Date(caseData.date);
                    const formattedDate = caseDate.toLocaleDateString('en-US', {
                        year: 'numeric',
                        month: '2-digit',
                        day: '2-digit'
                    }); // This will format as MM/DD/YYYY

                    const row = [
                        formattedDate,
                        caseData.id,
                        caseData.isTransfer ? 'Transfer' : caseData.type,
                        caseData.isTransfer ? 'N/A' : (caseData.queue || 'N/A'),
                        caseData.status || 'N/A',
                        caseData.isTransfer ? 'N/A' : (caseData.reasonCode || 'N/A'),
                        caseData.aht || '0',
                        caseData.asinCount || '0',
                        asinAdjustment
                    ];

                    // Properly escape fields that might contain commas
                    const escapedRow = row.map(field => {
                        if (field.toString().includes(',')) {
                            return `"${field}"`;
                        }
                        return field;
                    });

                    csvContent += escapedRow.join(',') + '\n';
                });

                // Get productive time data
                let productiveTimeInfo = '';
                if (selectedDate === new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0]) {
                    const productiveSeconds = (CaseSystem.auxTotals.dailyTotals.productive +
                                               (CaseSystem.getAuxCategory(CaseSystem.auxState.currentStatus) === 'productive' ?
                                                CaseSystem.auxTotals.productive : 0));

                    const hours = Math.floor(productiveSeconds / 3600);
                    const minutes = Math.floor((productiveSeconds % 3600) / 60);
                    productiveTimeInfo = `\n\nProductive Time: ${hours}h ${minutes}m`;
                } else {
                    const historicalData = GM_getValue(`auxData_${new Date(selectedDate).toLocaleDateString()}`);
                    if (historicalData) {
                        const data = JSON.parse(historicalData);
                        const hours = Math.floor(data.productive / 3600);
                        const minutes = Math.floor((data.productive % 3600) / 60);
                        productiveTimeInfo = `\n\nProductive Time: ${hours}h ${minutes}m`;
                    }
                }

                csvContent += productiveTimeInfo;

                // Create summary section
                const summary = `\nSummary Statistics
Total Cases: ${filteredCases.length}
Paragon Cases: ${filteredCases.filter(c => c.type === 'Paragon').length}
Photon Cases: ${filteredCases.filter(c => c.type === 'Photon').length}
Transfers: ${filteredCases.filter(c => c.isTransfer).length}
Total AHT: ${filteredCases.reduce((sum, c) => sum + (parseFloat(c.aht) || 0), 0).toFixed(1)} minutes`;

                csvContent += summary;

                // Create and trigger download
                const blob = new Blob([csvContent], { type: 'text/csv;charset=utf-8;' });
                const url = window.URL.createObjectURL(blob);
                const link = doc.createElement('a');
                link.setAttribute('href', url);
                link.setAttribute('download', `case_data_${selectedDate}.csv`);
                doc.body.appendChild(link);
                link.click();
                doc.body.removeChild(link);

                // Show success notification
                const notification = doc.createElement('div');
                notification.style.cssText = `
            position: fixed;
            top: 20px;
            left: 50%;
            transform: translateX(-50%);
            background: #4caf50;
            color: white;
            padding: 12px 24px;
            border-radius: 4px;
            z-index: 10000;
            font-size: 14px;
            box-shadow: 0 2px 8px rgba(0,0,0,0.2);
            animation: fadeInOut 3s ease-in-out;
        `;
                notification.textContent = 'Export completed successfully!';
                doc.body.appendChild(notification);

                setTimeout(() => notification.remove(), 3000);

            } catch (error) {
                console.error('Export error:', error);
                alert('Error exporting data: ' + error.message);
            }
        };

        // Add export button event listener
        const exportBtn = window.dashboardWindow.document.querySelector('.export-btn');
        if (exportBtn) {
            exportBtn.addEventListener('click', () => window.dashboardWindow.exportCaseData());
        }

        // Trigger file upload dialog
        window.dashboardWindow.triggerExcelUpload = function() {
            const input = window.dashboardWindow.document.getElementById('excelUploadInput');
            if (input) input.click();
        };

        const excelInput = window.dashboardWindow.document.getElementById('excelUploadInput');
        if (excelInput) {
            excelInput.addEventListener('change', function(e) {
                const file = e.target.files;
                if (!file) return;

                const statusDiv = window.dashboardWindow.document.getElementById('uploadStatus');
                statusDiv.innerHTML = '⏳ Reading Excel file...';
                statusDiv.style.color = '#007bff';

                const reader = new FileReader();
                reader.onload = function(event) {
                    try {
                        const data = new Uint8Array(event.target.result);
                        const workbook = XLSX.read(data, {type: 'array'});
                        const firstSheet = workbook.Sheets[workbook.SheetNames];
                        const jsonData = XLSX.utils.sheet_to_json(firstSheet);

                        // Process the Excel data
                        processExcelData(jsonData, statusDiv);
                    } catch (error) {
                        statusDiv.innerHTML = '❌ Error reading Excel file: ' + error.message;
                        statusDiv.style.color = '#dc3545';
                        console.error('Excel read error:', error);
                    }
                };
                reader.readAsArrayBuffer(file);

                // Reset input for re-upload
                e.target.value = '';
            });
        }

        // Process Excel data and update cases
        function processExcelData(excelData, statusDiv) {
            if (!excelData || excelData.length === 0) {
                statusDiv.innerHTML = '⚠️ No data found in Excel file';
                statusDiv.style.color = '#ffc107';
                return;
            }

            let updatedCount = 0;
            let notFoundCount = 0;
            const notFoundCases = [];

            statusDiv.innerHTML = `⏳ Processing ${excelData.length} cases...`;

            excelData.forEach(row => {
                const caseId = String(row['Case_ID'] || row['Case ID'] || row['CaseID'] || '').trim();
                const status = (row['Status'] || '').trim();
                const reasonCategory = (row['Reason_Category'] || row['Reason Category'] || '').trim();
                const reasonCode = (row['Reason_Code'] || row['Reason Code'] || '').trim();
                const blurb = row['Blurb (Case Specific)'] || row['Blurb'] || '';
                const annotation = row['Annotation'] || '';

                if (!caseId) return;

                if (CaseSystem.cases[caseId]) {
                    const caseData = CaseSystem.cases[caseId];

                    if (status) caseData.status = status;
                    if (reasonCategory) caseData.reasonCategory = reasonCategory;
                    if (reasonCode) caseData.reasonCode = reasonCode;
                    if (blurb) caseData.blurb = blurb;
                    if (annotation) caseData.annotation = annotation;

                    const statusLower = status.toLowerCase();
                    if (statusLower.includes('pending') ||
                        statusLower.includes('resolved') ||
                        statusLower.includes('closed')) {
                        if (!caseData.endTime) {
                            caseData.endTime = new Date().toISOString();
                        }
                    }

                    caseData.lastUpdated = new Date().toISOString();
                    caseData.updatedFromExcel = true;

                    updatedCount++;
                    console.log(`✅ Updated case ${caseId}: ${status}`);
                } else {
                    notFoundCount++;
                    notFoundCases.push(caseId);
                }
            });

            GM_setValue('cases', JSON.stringify(CaseSystem.cases));
            window.dashboardWindow.updateDashboardMetrics();
            window.dashboardWindow.updateCaseManagement();

            let resultHTML = `<strong>✅ Update Complete!</strong><br>`;
            resultHTML += `📊 Updated: <strong>${updatedCount}</strong> cases<br>`;

            if (notFoundCount > 0) {
                resultHTML += `⚠️ Not found: <strong>${notFoundCount}</strong> cases<br>`;
                if (notFoundCases.length <= 5) {
                    resultHTML += `<small style="color: #666;">Missing: ${notFoundCases.join(', ')}</small>`;
                }
            }

            statusDiv.innerHTML = resultHTML;
            statusDiv.style.color = '#28a745';

            const notification = window.dashboardWindow.document.createElement('div');
            notification.style.cssText = `
                position: fixed;
                top: 20px;
                left: 20px;
                padding: 15px 20px;
                background: #28a745;
                color: white;
                border-radius: 5px;
                box-shadow: 0 4px 6px rgba(0,0,0,0.3);
                z-index: 999999;
                font-size: 14px;
                font-weight: bold;
            `;
            notification.textContent = `✅ Excel Update: ${updatedCount} cases updated`;
            window.dashboardWindow.document.body.appendChild(notification);

            setTimeout(() => {
                notification.style.opacity = '0';
                notification.style.transition = 'opacity 0.3s';
                setTimeout(() => notification.remove(), 300);
            }, 4000);
        }
        // Add the debug function to the dashboard window

            console.log('All cases with dates:');
            Object.values(cases).forEach(caseData => {
                console.log({

                    parsedDate: new Date(caseData.date).toLocaleString()
                });

        };
        // Add the debug button to the table controls

            debugButton.textContent = 'Debug Dates';
            tableControls.appendChild(debugButton);
        }

        // Store original dashboard content
        const dashboardContent = window.dashboardWindow.document.querySelector('.dashboard-content');
        const originalDashboardContent = dashboardContent.innerHTML;

        // Add this new function
        async function initializeDashboard() {
            // Force immediate data refresh
            await CaseSystem.processCaseUpdates();
            await CaseSystem.loadStoredAUXData();

            // Update metrics immediately
            if (window.dashboardWindow && !window.dashboardWindow.closed) {
                window.dashboardWindow.updateDashboardMetrics();
                window.dashboardWindow.updateCaseManagement();
                CaseSystem.updateAuxDisplay();
            }

            // Initialize other components
            if (typeof QuickStats !== 'undefined') {
                QuickStats.init();
                QuickStats.update();
            }

            if (typeof AHTTracker !== 'undefined') {
                AHTTracker.lastMilestoneReached = 0;
            }

        }

        // Add refresh functionality to dashboard window
        window.dashboardWindow.refreshDashboard = async function() {
            const refreshBtn = this.document.querySelector('.refresh-btn');
            const loadingOverlay = this.document.querySelector('.loading-overlay');

            try {
                if (refreshBtn) refreshBtn.classList.add('refreshing');
                if (loadingOverlay) loadingOverlay.style.display = 'flex';

                // Store current OT month selection
                const currentOTMonth = this.selectedOTMonth;

                // Ensure data is fresh
                await CaseSystem.processCaseUpdates();
                CaseSystem.loadStoredAUXData();

                // Add this to update timestamps during refresh
                const today = new Date().toLocaleDateString();
                const auxData = JSON.parse(GM_getValue(`auxData_${today}`) || '{}');

                const startTimeElement = this.document.getElementById('startTime');
                const lastOfflineElement = this.document.getElementById('lastOffline');

                if (startTimeElement && auxData.firstAvailable) {
                    startTimeElement.textContent = new Date(auxData.firstAvailable)
                        .toLocaleTimeString('en-US', {
                        hour: '2-digit',
                        minute: '2-digit',
                        hour12: true
                    });
                }

                if (lastOfflineElement) {
                    if (CaseSystem.auxState.currentStatus.toLowerCase() === 'offline' && auxData.lastOffline) {
                        lastOfflineElement.textContent = new Date(auxData.lastOffline)
                            .toLocaleTimeString('en-US', {
                            hour: '2-digit',
                            minute: '2-digit',
                            hour12: true
                        });
                    } else {
                        lastOfflineElement.textContent = 'Currently Active';
                        lastOfflineElement.classList.add('active');
                    }
                }

                const now = new Date();
                const timeString = now.toLocaleTimeString();
                this.document.getElementById('lastUpdateTime').textContent = timeString;

                // Update all displays
                this.updateDashboardMetrics();
                this.updateCaseManagement();
                CaseSystem.updateAuxDisplay();
                // Update displays using stored selection
                this.updateOTDisplay(currentOTMonth);

                if (this.charts) {
                    this.updateCharts();
                }
                // Add this near the end


            } catch (error) {
                console.error('Error refreshing dashboard:', error);
            } finally {
                setTimeout(() => {
                    if (refreshBtn) refreshBtn.classList.remove('refreshing');
                    if (loadingOverlay) loadingOverlay.style.display = 'none';
                }, 500);
            }
        };

        // Update timestamp whenever dashboard is updated
        const originalUpdateDashboardMetrics = window.dashboardWindow.updateDashboardMetrics;
        window.dashboardWindow.updateDashboardMetrics = function() {
            originalUpdateDashboardMetrics.call(this);
            const now = new Date();
            const timeString = now.toLocaleTimeString();
            this.document.getElementById('lastUpdateTime').textContent = timeString;
        };

        window.dashboardWindow.updatePerformanceSummary = function() {
            try {
                const period = DASHBOARD_STATE.period;

                // Update button states first
                const doc = this.document;
                const weeklyBtn = doc.querySelector('.period-btn[data-period="weekly"]');
                const monthlyBtn = doc.querySelector('.period-btn[data-period="monthly"]');

                if (weeklyBtn && monthlyBtn) {
                    weeklyBtn.classList.remove('active');
                    monthlyBtn.classList.remove('active');

                    if (period === 'monthly') {
                        monthlyBtn.classList.add('active');
                    } else {
                        weeklyBtn.classList.add('active');
                    }
                }

                // Calculate date range
                const endDate = new Date();
                const startDate = new Date();
                if (period === 'weekly') {
                    startDate.setDate(endDate.getDate() - 7);
                } else {
                    startDate.setDate(endDate.getDate() - 30);
                }
                startDate.setHours(0, 0, 0, 0);
                endDate.setHours(23, 59, 59, 999);
                const data = {
                    period: {
                        totalCases: 0,
                        paragonCases: 0,
                        photonCases: 0,
                        transfers: 0,
                        aht: {
                            paragon: 0,
                            photon: 0,
                            overall: 0
                        }
                    },
                    total: {
                        totalCases: 0,
                        paragonCases: 0,
                        photonCases: 0,
                        transfers: 0,
                        aht: {
                            paragon: 0,
                            photon: 0,
                            overall: 0
                        }
                    }
                };

                // Calculate metrics for all cases
                Object.values(CaseSystem.cases).forEach(caseData => {
                    const caseDate = new Date(caseData.date);

                    // Update total counts
                    if (caseData.isTransfer) {
                        data.total.transfers++;
                        if (caseDate >= startDate && caseDate <= endDate) {
                            data.period.transfers++;
                        }
                    } else if (caseData.type === 'Paragon') {
                        data.total.paragonCases++;
                        if (caseDate >= startDate && caseDate <= endDate) {
                            data.period.paragonCases++;
                        }
                    } else if (caseData.type === 'Photon') {
                        data.total.photonCases++;
                        if (caseDate >= startDate && caseDate <= endDate) {
                            data.period.photonCases++;
                        }
                    }
                });

                // Calculate totals
                data.total.totalCases = data.total.paragonCases + data.total.photonCases + data.total.transfers;
                data.period.totalCases = data.period.paragonCases + data.period.photonCases + data.period.transfers;
                // Get period cases
                const periodCases = Object.values(CaseSystem.cases).filter(c => {
                    const caseDate = new Date(c.date);
                    return caseDate >= startDate && caseDate <= endDate;
                });

                // Calculate Total AHT instead of Average
                const ahtCalculations = {
                    paragon: periodCases
                    .filter(c => c.type === 'Paragon')
                    .reduce((sum, c) => sum + (parseFloat(c.aht) || 0), 0),
                    photon: periodCases
                    .filter(c => c.type === 'Photon')
                    .reduce((sum, c) => sum + (parseFloat(c.aht) || 0), 0),
                    transfers: periodCases
                    .filter(c => c.isTransfer)
                    .reduce((sum, c) => sum + 1.5, 0) // 1.5 for each transfer
                };

                // Calculate total AHT
                const totalAHT = ahtCalculations.paragon + ahtCalculations.photon + ahtCalculations.transfers;

                // Update DOM elements for AHT
                doc.getElementById('avgAHTSummary').textContent = totalAHT.toFixed(1);
                doc.getElementById('paragonAHTSummary').textContent = ahtCalculations.paragon.toFixed(1) + 'm';
                doc.getElementById('photonAHTSummary').textContent = ahtCalculations.photon.toFixed(1) + 'm';
                // Update case summary elements
                doc.getElementById('totalCasesSummary').textContent = data.period.totalCases;
                doc.getElementById('paragonCasesSummary').textContent = data.period.paragonCases;
                doc.getElementById('photonCasesSummary').textContent = data.period.photonCases;
                doc.getElementById('transfersCasesSummary').textContent = data.period.transfers;

                // Calculate AUX time
                const daysInPeriod = period === 'weekly' ? 7 : 30;
                const auxTotals = {
                    productive: Math.floor(CaseSystem.auxTotals.dailyTotals.productive +
                                           (CaseSystem.getAuxCategory(CaseSystem.auxState.currentStatus) === 'productive' ?
                                            CaseSystem.auxTotals.productive : 0)),
                    nonProductive: Math.floor(CaseSystem.auxTotals.dailyTotals.nonProductive +
                                              (CaseSystem.getAuxCategory(CaseSystem.auxState.currentStatus) === 'nonProductive' ?
                                               CaseSystem.auxTotals.nonProductive : 0)),
                    offline: Math.floor(CaseSystem.auxTotals.dailyTotals.offline +
                                        (CaseSystem.getAuxCategory(CaseSystem.auxState.currentStatus) === 'offline' ?
                                         CaseSystem.auxTotals.offline : 0))
                };

                // Update AUX display
                doc.getElementById('productiveTimeSummary').textContent = this.formatTime(auxTotals.productive);
                doc.getElementById('nonProductiveTimeSummary').textContent = this.formatTime(auxTotals.nonProductive);
                doc.getElementById('offlineTimeSummary').textContent = this.formatTime(auxTotals.offline);
                // Complete chart update section
                if (this.performanceCharts) {
                    const dates = [];
                    const currentDate = new Date(startDate);
                    while (currentDate <= endDate) {
                        dates.push(new Date(currentDate));
                        currentDate.setDate(currentDate.getDate() + 1);
                    }

                    // Calculate efficiency for each day
                    const dailyEfficiencies = dates.map(date => {
                        const dayStart = new Date(date);
                        dayStart.setHours(0, 0, 0, 0);
                        const dayEnd = new Date(date);
                        dayEnd.setHours(23, 59, 59, 999);

                        const dayCases = Object.values(CaseSystem.cases).filter(c => {
                            const caseDate = new Date(c.date);
                            return caseDate >= dayStart && caseDate <= dayEnd;
                        });

                        // Calculate total AHT for the day
                        const dayTotalAHT = dayCases.reduce((sum, c) => {
                            return sum + (c.isTransfer ? 1.5 : (parseFloat(c.aht) || 0));
                        }, 0);

                        // Get productive minutes for the day
                        const dayProductiveMinutes = Math.floor(auxTotals.productive / 60);

                        // Calculate daily efficiency
                        return dayProductiveMinutes > 0 ? (dayTotalAHT / dayProductiveMinutes) * 100 : 0;
                    });

                    // Calculate average efficiency from daily efficiencies
                    const validEfficiencies = dailyEfficiencies.filter(eff => eff > 0);
                    const averageEfficiency = validEfficiencies.length > 0
                    ? validEfficiencies.reduce((sum, eff) => sum + eff, 0) / validEfficiencies.length
                    : 0;

                    // Update Average Daily Efficiency
                    const efficiencyElement = doc.getElementById('avgEfficiencySummary');
                    efficiencyElement.textContent = averageEfficiency.toFixed(1) + '%';
                    efficiencyElement.style.color =
                        averageEfficiency > 150 ? '#d13212' :
                    averageEfficiency > 100 ? '#ff9900' :
                    averageEfficiency >= 90 ? '#4caf50' :
                    '#ff9900';

                    // Format date labels
                    const dateLabels = dates.map(date =>
                                                 period === 'weekly'
                                                 ? date.toLocaleDateString('en-US', { weekday: 'short', month: 'numeric', day: 'numeric' })
                                                 : date.toLocaleDateString('en-US', { month: 'short', day: 'numeric' })
                                                );

                    // Update Daily Cases Chart
                    const dailyCaseData = dates.map(date => {
                        const dayStart = new Date(date);
                        dayStart.setHours(0, 0, 0, 0);
                        const dayEnd = new Date(date);
                        dayEnd.setHours(23, 59, 59, 999);

                        const dayCases = Object.values(CaseSystem.cases).filter(c => {
                            const caseDate = new Date(c.date);
                            return caseDate >= dayStart && caseDate <= dayEnd;
                        });

                        return {
                            paragon: dayCases.filter(c => c.type === 'Paragon').length,
                            photon: dayCases.filter(c => c.type === 'Photon').length,
                            transfers: dayCases.filter(c => c.isTransfer).length
                        };
                    });

                    this.performanceCharts.dailyCases.data.labels = dateLabels;
                    this.performanceCharts.dailyCases.data.datasets[0].data = dailyCaseData.map(d => d.transfers);
                    this.performanceCharts.dailyCases.data.datasets[1].data = dailyCaseData.map(d => d.photon);
                    this.performanceCharts.dailyCases.data.datasets[2].data = dailyCaseData.map(d => d.paragon);

                    // Adjust scale for daily cases chart
                    const maxCases = Math.max(
                        ...dailyCaseData.map(d => d.paragon + d.photon + d.transfers)
                    );
                    this.performanceCharts.dailyCases.options.scales.y.suggestedMax =
                        Math.ceil(maxCases * 1.2);
                    this.performanceCharts.dailyCases.update();

                    // Update Efficiency Trend chart
                    this.performanceCharts.efficiency.data.labels = dateLabels;
                    this.performanceCharts.efficiency.data.datasets[0].data = dailyEfficiencies;

                    // Adjust scale for efficiency chart
                    const maxEfficiency = Math.max(...dailyEfficiencies);
                    this.performanceCharts.efficiency.options.scales.y.suggestedMax =
                        Math.ceil(maxEfficiency * 1.2);
                    this.performanceCharts.efficiency.update();

                    // Debug logging
                    console.log('Chart Updates:', {
                        period: period,
                        dateRange: {
                            start: startDate.toISOString(),
                            end: endDate.toISOString()
                        },
                        metrics: {
                            totalCases: data.period.totalCases,
                            averageEfficiency: averageEfficiency,
                            maxDailyCases: maxCases,
                            maxEfficiency: maxEfficiency
                        },
                        dailyData: dateLabels.map((date, i) => ({
                            date: date,
                            cases: dailyCaseData[i],
                            efficiency: dailyEfficiencies[i]
                        }))
                    });
                }


                console.log('Performance Summary Update:', {
                    period: period,
                    dateRange: {
                        start: startDate.toISOString(),
                        end: endDate.toISOString()
                    },
                    metrics: {
                        totalCases: data.period.totalCases,
                        totalAHT: totalAHT,
                        averageEfficiency: averageEfficiency
                    }
                });

            } catch (error) {
                console.error('Error updating performance summary:', error);
            }
        };

        // Add period button initialization
        function initializePeriodButtons() {
            const doc = window.dashboardWindow.document;
            const buttons = doc.querySelectorAll('.period-btn');

            buttons.forEach(button => {
                button.addEventListener('click', function() {
                    // Remove active class from all buttons
                    buttons.forEach(btn => btn.classList.remove('active'));
                    // Add active class to clicked button
                    this.classList.add('active');
                    // Update summary with selected period
                    window.dashboardWindow.updatePerformanceSummary(this.dataset.period);
                });
            });
        }


        // Helper function for time formatting
        window.dashboardWindow.formatTime = function(seconds) {
            const hours = Math.floor(seconds / 3600);
            const minutes = Math.floor((seconds % 3600) / 60);
            return `${hours}h ${minutes}m`;
        };

        // In your openDashboard function, after writing the HTML:
        window.dashboardWindow.document.write(allStyles);
        window.dashboardWindow.document.close();
        window.dashboardWindow.updateCaseManagement = async function() {
            // Force data refresh when function is called
            await CaseSystem.processCaseUpdates();

            const cases = CaseSystem.cases;
            const tbody = this.document.getElementById('caseTableBody');
            if (!tbody) {
                console.error('Could not find caseTableBody element');
                return;
            }

            try {
                // Show loading indicator
                const loadingIndicator = this.document.createElement('div');
                loadingIndicator.className = 'loading-indicator';
                loadingIndicator.innerHTML = 'Loading cases...';
                tbody.parentElement.insertBefore(loadingIndicator, tbody);

                // Get selected date (default to today)
                const selectedDate = this.document.getElementById('selectedDate')?.value ||
                      new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0];

                // Get other filter values
                const caseType = this.document.getElementById('caseTypeFilter')?.value;
                const queueFilter = this.document.getElementById('queueFilter')?.value;

                // Filter cases for selected date
                const filteredCases = Object.values(cases).filter(caseData => {
                    const caseDate = new Date(caseData.date).toISOString().split('T')[0];

                    // First filter by date
                    if (caseDate !== selectedDate) return false;

                    // Then apply other filters
                    if (caseType && caseData.type !== caseType &&
                        !(caseData.isTransfer && caseType === 'Transfer')) return false;
                    if (queueFilter && caseData.queue !== queueFilter &&
                        !caseData.isTransfer) return false;

                    return true;
                });

                // Sort cases by time
                filteredCases.sort((a, b) => new Date(b.date) - new Date(a.date));

                // Clear existing content and update
                tbody.innerHTML = filteredCases.map(caseData => `
        <tr class="${caseData.isTransfer ? 'transfer-row' : ''}" data-case-id="${caseData.id}">
            <td>${new Date(caseData.date).toLocaleTimeString()}</td>
            <td>
                <a href="${CaseSystem.generateParagonUrl(caseData.id, caseData.queue)}"
                   class="case-id-link"
                   target="_blank"
                   title="Open in ${CaseSystem.getParagonEnvironment(caseData.queue).toUpperCase()} Paragon">
                    ${caseData.originalCaseId || caseData.id}
                    <span class="material-icons" style="font-size: 14px; margin-left: 4px;">
                        open_in_new
                    </span>
                </a>
            </td>
            <td>${caseData.isTransfer ? 'Transfer' : caseData.type}</td>
            <td>${caseData.isTransfer ? 'N/A' : (caseData.queue || 'N/A')}</td>
            <td>${caseData.status || 'N/A'}</td>
            <td>${caseData.isTransfer ? 'N/A' : (caseData.reasonCode || 'N/A')}</td>
            <td>${caseData.aht || 0}
                ${caseData.asinCount > 3 ?
                                                    `<span class="asin-badge" title="${caseData.asinCount} ASINs">
                        +${((caseData.asinCount - 3) * 30 / 60).toFixed(1)}m
                    </span>` :
                                                    ''}
            </td>
        </tr>
    `).join('');

                // Add the styles
                if (!this.document.getElementById('case-link-styles')) {
                    const styleElement = this.document.createElement('style');
                    styleElement.id = 'case-link-styles';
                    styleElement.textContent = `
            .case-id-link {
                color: #2196f3;
                text-decoration: none;
                font-family: 'Monaco', monospace;
                display: inline-flex;
                align-items: center;
                padding: 4px 8px;
                border-radius: 4px;
                transition: all 0.2s ease;
            }

            .case-id-link:hover {
                background: rgba(33, 150, 243, 0.1);
                color: #1976d2;
            }

            .case-id-link .material-icons {
                opacity: 0;
                transition: opacity 0.2s ease;
            }

            .case-id-link:hover .material-icons {
                opacity: 1;
            }
        `;
                    this.document.head.appendChild(styleElement);
                }


                const displayDate = this.document.getElementById('displayDate');
                const dateSpecificCount = this.document.getElementById('dateSpecificCount');

                function getProductiveTimeClass(hours) {
                    return hours >= 8 ? 'pt-achieved' : 'pt-pending';
                }

                if (selectedDate === new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0]) {
                    displayDate.textContent = "Today's Cases";

                    // Get productive time for today with real-time update
                    const today = new Date().toLocaleDateString();
                    const productiveSeconds = (CaseSystem.auxTotals.dailyTotals.productive +
                                               (CaseSystem.getAuxCategory(CaseSystem.auxState.currentStatus) === 'productive' ?
                                                CaseSystem.auxTotals.productive : 0));

                    const productiveTime = {
                        hours: Math.floor(productiveSeconds / 3600),
                        minutes: Math.floor((productiveSeconds % 3600) / 60)
                    };

                    dateSpecificCount.innerHTML = `
                <span class="productive-time ${getProductiveTimeClass(productiveTime.hours)}">
                    ${productiveTime.hours}h ${productiveTime.minutes}m
                </span>
                <span class="case-count">${filteredCases.length} cases</span>
            `;
                } else {
                    displayDate.textContent = new Date(selectedDate).toLocaleDateString();

                    // Get historical productive time
                    const historicalData = GM_getValue(`auxData_${new Date(selectedDate).toLocaleDateString()}`);
                    let ptDisplay = '';

                    if (historicalData) {
                        const data = JSON.parse(historicalData);
                        const hours = Math.floor(data.productive / 3600);
                        const minutes = Math.floor((data.productive % 3600) / 60);
                        ptDisplay = `
                    <span class="productive-time ${getProductiveTimeClass(hours)}">
                        ${hours}h ${minutes}m
                    </span>
                `;
                    }

                    dateSpecificCount.innerHTML = `
                ${ptDisplay}
                <span class="case-count">${filteredCases.length} cases</span>
            `;
                }

                // Update filter status
                const filterStatus = this.document.getElementById('filterStatus');
                if (filterStatus) {
                    const totalDayCases = Object.values(cases).filter(c =>
                                                                      new Date(c.date).toISOString().split('T')[0] === selectedDate
                                                                     ).length;

                    filterStatus.textContent = `Showing ${filteredCases.length} of ${totalDayCases} cases for this date`;
                }

                // Remove loading indicator
                if (loadingIndicator) {
                    loadingIndicator.remove();
                }

                // Set up automatic refresh
                if (!this.caseManagementRefreshInterval) {
                    this.caseManagementRefreshInterval = setInterval(() => {
                        const activeTab = this.document.querySelector('.nav-tabs button.active');
                        if (activeTab && activeTab.textContent.includes('Case Details')) {
                            this.updateCaseManagement();
                        } else {
                            // Clear interval if we're not on the Case Details tab
                            clearInterval(this.caseManagementRefreshInterval);
                            this.caseManagementRefreshInterval = null;
                        }
                    }, 5000); // Refresh every 5 seconds
                }

                console.log('Case management updated successfully:', {
                    date: selectedDate,
                    casesCount: filteredCases.length,
                    filters: { caseType, queueFilter }
                });

            } catch (error) {
                console.error('Error updating case management:', error);
                if (loadingIndicator) {
                    loadingIndicator.remove();
                }
            }
        };

        window.dashboardWindow.initializeDateSelector = function() {
            const datePicker = this.document.getElementById('selectedDate');
            if (!datePicker) return;

            // Set default to today
            const today = new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0];
            datePicker.value = today;

            // Add change listener
            datePicker.addEventListener('change', (e) => {
                // Force immediate update when date changes
                this.updateCaseManagement();

                // Add a small delay to ensure data is properly loaded
                setTimeout(() => {
                    this.updateCaseManagement();
                }, 100);
            });
        };



        // Add queue filter options update function
        window.dashboardWindow.updateQueueFilterOptions = function(cases) {
            const queueFilter = this.document.getElementById('queueFilter');
            if (queueFilter && queueFilter.options.length === 1) {
                const queues = new Set();
                Object.values(cases).forEach(caseData => {
                    if (caseData.queue && !caseData.isTransfer) {
                        queues.add(caseData.queue);
                    }
                });
                [...queues].sort().forEach(queue => {
                    const option = document.createElement('option');
                    option.value = queue;
                    option.textContent = queue;
                    queueFilter.appendChild(option);
                });
            }
        };
        window.dashboardWindow.initializeFilterOptions = function() {
            const cases = CaseSystem.cases;

            // Initialize Queue Filter
            const queueFilterElement = this.document.getElementById('queueFilter');
            if (queueFilterElement) {
                // Clear existing options except the first one (All Queues)
                while (queueFilterElement.options.length > 1) {
                    queueFilterElement.remove(1);
                }

                // Add queue options
                const queues = new Set();
                Object.values(cases).forEach(caseData => {
                    if (caseData.queue && !caseData.isTransfer) {
                        queues.add(caseData.queue);
                    }
                });
                [...queues].sort().forEach(queue => {
                    const option = document.createElement('option');
                    option.value = queue;
                    option.textContent = queue;
                    queueFilterElement.appendChild(option);
                });
            }

            // Initialize Case Type Filter
            const caseTypeFilterElement = this.document.getElementById('caseTypeFilter');
            if (caseTypeFilterElement) {
                // Clear existing options except the first one (All Types)
                while (caseTypeFilterElement.options.length > 1) {
                    caseTypeFilterElement.remove(1);
                }

                // Add case type options
                const types = new Set(['Paragon', 'Photon', 'Transfer']);
                [...types].sort().forEach(type => {
                    const option = document.createElement('option');
                    option.value = type;
                    option.textContent = type;
                    caseTypeFilterElement.appendChild(option);
                });
            }
        };


        // Add filter handling functions
        window.dashboardWindow.applyFilters = function() {
            this.updateCaseManagement();
        };

        window.dashboardWindow.clearFilters = function() {
            const doc = this.document;
            doc.getElementById('dateFrom').value = '';
            doc.getElementById('dateTo').value = '';
            doc.getElementById('caseTypeFilter').value = '';
            doc.getElementById('queueFilter').value = '';
            this.updateCaseManagement();
        };
        window.dashboardWindow.initializeAnalytics = function() {
            const analyticsDatePicker = this.document.getElementById('analyticsDatePicker');
            if (analyticsDatePicker) {
                analyticsDatePicker.addEventListener('change', (e) => {
                    this.updateCharts(e.target.value);
                });
            }
        };

        window.dashboardWindow.initializeScorecard = function() {
            const scorecardMonthPicker = this.document.getElementById('scorecardMonthPicker');

            // Calculate correct default month based on current date
            const today = new Date();
            let defaultMonth;

            if (today.getDate() <= 20) {
                // If before the 20th, use previous month
                defaultMonth = `${today.getFullYear()}-${String(today.getMonth()).padStart(2, '0')}`;
            } else {
                // If after the 20th, use current month
                defaultMonth = `${today.getFullYear()}-${String(today.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0')}`;
            }

            scorecardMonthPicker.value = defaultMonth;

            // Add change listener
            scorecardMonthPicker.addEventListener('change', (e) => {
                this.updateScorecard(e.target.value);
            });

            this.scorecardInitialized = true;
            this.updateScorecard(defaultMonth); // Initial update with correct month
        };


        // Helper function to check if date is in scorecard range (21st - 20th)
        function isWithinScoreCardRange(date, selectedMonth = null) {
            const checkDate = new Date(date);
            let startDate, endDate;

            if (selectedMonth) {
                // Parse selected month (format: "YYYY-MM")
                const [year, month] = selectedMonth.split('-').map(Number);
                startDate = new Date(year, month - 1, 21); // 21st of selected month
                endDate = new Date(year, month, 20); // 20th of next month
            } else {
                // Current month range
                const today = new Date();
                if (today.getDate() <= 20) {
                    // If today is 20th or earlier, use previous month's 21st to today's 20th
                    startDate = new Date(today.getFullYear(), today.getMonth() - 1, 21);
                    endDate = new Date(today.getFullYear(), today.getMonth(), 20);
                } else {
                    // If today is after 20th, use current month's 21st to next month's 20th
                    startDate = new Date(today.getFullYear(), today.getMonth(), 21);
                    endDate = new Date(today.getFullYear(), today.getMonth() + 1, 20);
                }
            }

            return checkDate >= startDate && checkDate <= endDate;
        }
        window.dashboardWindow.updateScoreCardPeriodDisplay = function(selectedMonth = null) {
            const displayElement = this.document.getElementById('scorecardDisplayDate');

            if (!displayElement) return;

            if (selectedMonth) {
                // Parse selected month (format: "YYYY-MM")
                const [year, month] = selectedMonth.split('-').map(Number);

                // Get previous month for start date (21st)
                const startDate = new Date(year, month - 1, 21);
                // Get selected month for end date (20th)
                const endDate = new Date(year, month, 20);

                const startMonthName = startDate.toLocaleString('default', { month: 'short' });
                const endMonthName = endDate.toLocaleString('default', { month: 'short' });

                displayElement.textContent =
                    `Period: ${startMonthName} 21 - ${endMonthName} 20, ${year}`;
            } else {
                // Current period logic
                const today = new Date();
                const currentDay = today.getDate();

                let startDate, endDate;
                if (currentDay <= 20) {
                    // If today is 20th or earlier
                    startDate = new Date(today.getFullYear(), today.getMonth() - 1, 21);
                    endDate = new Date(today.getFullYear(), today.getMonth(), 20);
                } else {
                    // If today is after 20th
                    startDate = new Date(today.getFullYear(), today.getMonth(), 21);
                    endDate = new Date(today.getFullYear(), today.getMonth() + 1, 20);
                }

                const startMonthName = startDate.toLocaleString('default', { month: 'short' });
                const endMonthName = endDate.toLocaleString('default', { month: 'short' });

                displayElement.textContent =
                    `Period: ${startMonthName} 21 - ${endMonthName} 20, ${startDate.getFullYear()}`;
            }
        };
        window.dashboardWindow.updateScorecardCharts = function(metrics) {
            if (this.scorecardCharts?.caseDistribution) {
                this.scorecardCharts.caseDistribution.data.datasets[0].data = [
                    metrics.paragon.regular.count,
                    metrics.paragon.hsi.count,
                    Object.values(metrics.photon.regular).reduce((sum, data) => sum + data.count, 0),
                    Object.values(metrics.photon.sme).reduce((sum, data) => sum + data.count, 0),
                    metrics.transfers.total
                ];
                this.scorecardCharts.caseDistribution.update();
            }

            // Add AHT chart update
            if (this.scorecardCharts?.ahtComparison) {
                const photonRegularAHT = Object.values(metrics.photon.regular)
                .reduce((sum, data) => sum + data.aht, 0);
                const photonSMEAHT = Object.values(metrics.photon.sme)
                .reduce((sum, data) => sum + data.aht, 0);

                this.scorecardCharts.ahtComparison.data.datasets[0].data = [
                    metrics.paragon.regular.aht,
                    metrics.paragon.hsi.aht,
                    photonRegularAHT,
                    photonSMEAHT,
                    metrics.transfers.aht
                ];
                this.scorecardCharts.ahtComparison.update();
            }
        };

        window.dashboardWindow.updateScorecard = function(selectedMonth = null) {
            const cases = CaseSystem.cases;

            // Initialize counters
            const metrics = {
                paragon: {
                    total: 0,
                    totalAHT: 0,
                    regular: { count: 0, aht: 0 },
                    hsi: { count: 0, aht: 0 }
                },
                photon: {
                    total: 0,
                    totalAHT: 0,
                    regular: {},
                    sme: {}
                },
                transfers: {
                    total: 0,
                    aht: 0
                }
            };

            // Filter and process cases
            Object.values(cases)
                .filter(caseData => isWithinScoreCardRange(caseData.date, selectedMonth))
                .forEach(caseData => {
                if (caseData.isTransfer) {
                    metrics.transfers.total++;
                    metrics.transfers.aht += 1.5; // Standard transfer AHT
                }
                else if (caseData.type === 'Paragon') {
                    metrics.paragon.total++;
                    metrics.paragon.totalAHT += parseFloat(caseData.aht) || 0;

                    // Check if HSI queue
                    if (caseData.queue && caseData.queue.toLowerCase().includes('hsi')) {
                        metrics.paragon.hsi.count++;
                        metrics.paragon.hsi.aht += parseFloat(caseData.aht) || 0;
                    } else {
                        metrics.paragon.regular.count++;
                        metrics.paragon.regular.aht += parseFloat(caseData.aht) || 0;
                    }
                }
                else if (caseData.type === 'Photon') {
                    metrics.photon.total++;
                    metrics.photon.totalAHT += parseFloat(caseData.aht) || 0;

                    const category = caseData.queue.toLowerCase().includes('sme') ? 'sme' : 'regular';
                    const uowType = caseData.status || 'Unknown';

                    // Initialize UoW type if not exists
                    if (!metrics.photon[category][uowType]) {
                        metrics.photon[category][uowType] = { count: 0, aht: 0 };
                    }

                    metrics.photon[category][uowType].count++;
                    metrics.photon[category][uowType].aht += parseFloat(caseData.aht) || 0;
                }
            });

            // Update display
            this.updateScorecardDisplay(metrics);
            // Update the period display with selected month
            this.updateScoreCardPeriodDisplay(selectedMonth);
            this.updateScorecardCharts(metrics);
        };
        window.dashboardWindow.updateScorecardDisplay = function(metrics) {
            const doc = this.document;

            // Update Paragon Card
            doc.getElementById('paragonTotal').textContent = metrics.paragon.total;
            // Total AHT instead of average
            doc.getElementById('paragonAHT').textContent =
                `${metrics.paragon.totalAHT.toFixed(1)}m`;

            doc.getElementById('regularCount').textContent = metrics.paragon.regular.count;
            // Total AHT for regular cases
            doc.getElementById('regularAHT').textContent =
                `${metrics.paragon.regular.aht.toFixed(1)}m`;

            doc.getElementById('hsiCount').textContent = metrics.paragon.hsi.count;
            // Total AHT for HSI cases
            doc.getElementById('hsiAHT').textContent =
                `${metrics.paragon.hsi.aht.toFixed(1)}m`;

            // Update Photon Card
            doc.getElementById('photonTotal').textContent = metrics.photon.total;
            // Total AHT for Photon
            doc.getElementById('photonAHT').textContent =
                `${metrics.photon.totalAHT.toFixed(1)}m`;

            // Update UoW breakdowns with total AHT
            const regularUowBreakdown = doc.getElementById('regularUowBreakdown');
            const smeUowBreakdown = doc.getElementById('smeUowBreakdown');

            regularUowBreakdown.innerHTML = this.generateUowBreakdownHTML(metrics.photon.regular);
            smeUowBreakdown.innerHTML = this.generateUowBreakdownHTML(metrics.photon.sme);

            // Update Transfers Card
            doc.getElementById('transferTotal').textContent = metrics.transfers.total;
            // Total transfer AHT
            doc.getElementById('transferBreakdown').textContent =
                `Total AHT: ${metrics.transfers.aht.toFixed(1)}m`;

            // Update period display
            this.updateScoreCardPeriodDisplay();
        };

        // Update UoW breakdown to show total AHT
        window.dashboardWindow.generateUowBreakdownHTML = function(uowData) {
            return Object.entries(uowData)
                .map(([uowType, data]) => `
            <div class="uow-item">
                <div class="uow-name">${uowType}</div>
                <div class="uow-stats">
                    Count: ${data.count}
                    <div class="uow-aht">AHT: ${data.aht.toFixed(1)}m</div>
                </div>
            </div>
        `).join('');
        };
