        window.dashboardWindow.initializeExportFeatures = function() {
            const exportBtn = this.document.querySelector('.scorecard-export-btn');
            if (exportBtn) {
                exportBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
                    console.log('Scorecard Export button clicked');
                    this.exportScorecard();
                });
            }
        };
        // Add this chart initialization to your initializeScorecard function
        window.dashboardWindow.initializeScorecardCharts = function() {
            console.log('Initializing Scorecard Charts');
            const canvas = this.document.getElementById('caseDistributionChart');
            if (!canvas) {
                console.error('Could not find chart canvas element');
                return;
            }
            const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
            console.log('Chart context:', ctx);


            this.scorecardCharts = {
                caseDistribution: new Chart(ctx, {
                    type: 'bar',
                    data: {
                        labels: ['Paragon Regular', 'Paragon HSI', 'Photon Regular', 'Photon SME', 'Transfers'],
                        datasets: [{
                            data: [0, 0, 0, 0, 0],
                            backgroundColor: [
                                'rgba(35, 47, 62, 0.8)',    // Paragon Regular
                                'rgba(35, 47, 62, 0.6)',    // Paragon HSI
                                'rgba(255, 153, 0, 0.8)',   // Photon Regular
                                'rgba(255, 153, 0, 0.6)',   // Photon SME
                                'rgba(25, 118, 210, 0.8)'   // Transfers
                            ],
                            borderColor: [
                                'rgba(35, 47, 62, 1)',
                                'rgba(35, 47, 62, 1)',
                                'rgba(255, 153, 0, 1)',
                                'rgba(255, 153, 0, 1)',
                                'rgba(25, 118, 210, 1)'
                            ],
                            borderWidth: 1,
                            borderRadius: 6
                        }]
                    },
                    options: {
                        responsive: true,
                        maintainAspectRatio: false,
                        plugins: {
                            legend: {
                                display: false
                            },
                            title: {
                                display: true,
                                text: 'Case Distribution',
                                color: '#232f3e',
                                font: {
                                    size: 16,
                                    weight: 600
                                }
                            },
                            tooltip: {
                                callbacks: {
                                    label: function(context) {
                                        return `Count: ${context.raw}`;
                                    }
                                }
                            }
                        },
                        scales: {
                            y: {
                                beginAtZero: true,
                                grid: {
                                    drawBorder: false,
                                    color: 'rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.05)'
                                },
                                ticks: {
                                    font: {
                                        size: 12
                                    }
                                }
                            },
                            x: {
                                grid: {
                                    display: false
                                },
                                ticks: {
                                    font: {
                                        size: 12
                                    }
                                }
                            }
                        }
                    }
                })
            };
            // Add AHT Chart
            const ahtCtx = this.document.getElementById('ahtComparisonChart').getContext('2d');

            this.scorecardCharts.ahtComparison = new Chart(ahtCtx, {
                type: 'bar',
                data: {
                    labels: ['Paragon Regular', 'Paragon HSI', 'Photon Regular', 'Photon SME', 'Transfers'],
                    datasets: [{
                        label: 'Total AHT (minutes)',
                        data: [0, 0, 0, 0, 0],
                        backgroundColor: [
                            'rgba(35, 47, 62, 0.8)',    // Paragon Regular
                            'rgba(35, 47, 62, 0.6)',    // Paragon HSI
                            'rgba(255, 153, 0, 0.8)',   // Photon Regular
                            'rgba(255, 153, 0, 0.6)',   // Photon SME
                            'rgba(25, 118, 210, 0.8)'   // Transfers
                        ],
                        borderColor: [
                            'rgba(35, 47, 62, 1)',
                            'rgba(35, 47, 62, 1)',
                            'rgba(255, 153, 0, 1)',
                            'rgba(255, 153, 0, 1)',
                            'rgba(25, 118, 210, 1)'
                        ],
                        borderWidth: 1,
                        borderRadius: 6
                    }]
                },
                options: {
                    responsive: true,
                    maintainAspectRatio: false,
                    plugins: {
                        legend: {
                            display: false
                        },
                        tooltip: {
                            callbacks: {
                                label: function(context) {
                                    return `Total AHT: ${context.raw.toFixed(1)}m`;
                                }
                            }
                        }
                    },
                    scales: {
                        y: {
                            beginAtZero: true,
                            grid: {
                                drawBorder: false,
                                color: 'rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.05)'
                            },
                            ticks: {
                                callback: function(value) {
                                    return value + 'm';
                                },
                                font: {
                                    size: 12
                                }
                            }
                        },
                        x: {
                            grid: {
                                display: false
                            },
                            ticks: {
                                font: {
                                    size: 12
                                }
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
            });
        };


        window.dashboardWindow.exportScorecard = function() {
            console.log('Scorecard Export process started');

            try {
                // Add SheetJS library if not already added
                if (!window.XLSX) {
                    const script = document.createElement('script');
                    script.src = 'https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/xlsx/dist/xlsx.full.min.js';
                    document.head.appendChild(script);

                    script.onload = () => this.generateExcel();
                } else {
                    this.generateExcel();
                }
            } catch (error) {
                console.error('Scorecard Export error:', error);
                alert('Error exporting scorecard: ' + error.message);
            }
        };

        window.dashboardWindow.generateExcel = function() {
            try {
                const selectedMonth = this.document.getElementById('scorecardMonthPicker').value;
                const metrics = this.calculateScorecardMetrics(selectedMonth);

                // Create workbook
                const wb = XLSX.utils.book_new();

                // SHEET 1: Summary Statistics
                const summaryData = [
                    ['SCORECARD STATS'],
                    [this.document.getElementById('scorecardDisplayDate').textContent],
                    [''],
                    ['PARAGON CASES'],
                    ['Total Cases', metrics.paragon.total],
                    ['Total AHT', `${metrics.paragon.totalAHT.toFixed(1)}m`],
                    [''],
                    ['Regular Cases'],
                    ['Count', metrics.paragon.regular.count],
                    ['AHT', `${metrics.paragon.regular.aht.toFixed(1)}m`],
                    [''],
                    ['HSI Cases'],
                    ['Count', metrics.paragon.hsi.count],
                    ['AHT', `${metrics.paragon.hsi.aht.toFixed(1)}m`],
                    [''],
                    ['PHOTON CASES'],
                    ['Total Cases', metrics.photon.total],
                    ['Total AHT', `${metrics.photon.totalAHT.toFixed(1)}m`],
                    [''],
                    ['Regular UoW Breakdown'],
                    ['UoW Type', 'Count', 'AHT']
                ];

                // Add Regular UoW data
                Object.entries(metrics.photon.regular).forEach(([uowType, data]) => {
                    summaryData.push([uowType, data.count, `${data.aht.toFixed(1)}m`]);
                });

                summaryData.push(
                    [''],
                    ['SME UoW Breakdown'],
                    ['UoW Type', 'Count', 'AHT']
                );

                // Add SME UoW data
                Object.entries(metrics.photon.sme).forEach(([uowType, data]) => {
                    summaryData.push([uowType, data.count, `${data.aht.toFixed(1)}m`]);
                });

                summaryData.push(
                    [''],
                    ['TRANSFERS'],
                    ['Total Cases', metrics.transfers.total],
                    ['Total AHT', `${metrics.transfers.aht.toFixed(1)}m`]
                );

                // Create Summary Sheet
                const ws1 = XLSX.utils.aoa_to_sheet(summaryData);
                XLSX.utils.book_append_sheet(wb, ws1, 'Summary Stats');

                // SHEET 2: Case Details
                const caseHeaders = [['Date', 'Time', 'Case ID', 'Type', 'Queue', 'Status', 'Reason Code', 'AHT (min)']];
                const filteredCases = Object.values(CaseSystem.cases)
                .filter(caseData => isWithinScoreCardRange(caseData.date, selectedMonth))
                .sort((a, b) => new Date(b.date) - new Date(a.date))
                .map(caseData => {
                    const caseDate = new Date(caseData.date);
                    return [
                        caseDate.toLocaleDateString(),
                        caseDate.toLocaleTimeString(),
                        caseData.id,
                        caseData.isTransfer ? 'Transfer' : caseData.type,
                        caseData.isTransfer ? 'N/A' : (caseData.queue || 'N/A'),
                        caseData.status || 'N/A',
                        caseData.isTransfer ? 'N/A' : (caseData.reasonCode || 'N/A'),
                        caseData.aht || '0'
                    ];
                });

                const caseData = [...caseHeaders, ...filteredCases];
                const ws2 = XLSX.utils.aoa_to_sheet(caseData);
                XLSX.utils.book_append_sheet(wb, ws2, 'Case Details');

                // Generate Excel file
                const fileName = `scorecard_${selectedMonth || 'current'}_${new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0]}.xlsx`;
                XLSX.writeFile(wb, fileName);

                // Show success notification
                this.showExportNotification('Scorecard exported successfully!');
                console.log('Export completed successfully');

            } catch (error) {
                console.error('Excel generation error:', error);
                alert('Error generating Excel file: ' + error.message);
            }
        };

        // Add event listener setup to your initialization
        if (window.dashboardWindow.document.querySelector('.scorecard-export-btn')) {
            window.dashboardWindow.document.querySelector('.scorecard-export-btn')
                .addEventListener('click', () => window.dashboardWindow.exportScorecard());
        }


        window.dashboardWindow.calculateScorecardMetrics = function(selectedMonth) {
            const cases = CaseSystem.cases;

            // Initialize metrics structure
            const metrics = {
                paragon: {
                    total: 0,
                    totalAHT: 0,
                    regular: { count: 0, aht: 0 },
                    hsi: { count: 0, aht: 0 }
                },
                photon: {
                    total: 0,
                    totalAHT: 0,
                    regular: {},
                    sme: {}
                },
                transfers: {
                    total: 0,
                    aht: 0
                }
            };

            // Filter and process cases
            Object.values(cases)
                .filter(caseData => isWithinScoreCardRange(caseData.date, selectedMonth))
                .forEach(caseData => {
                if (caseData.isTransfer) {
                    metrics.transfers.total++;
                    metrics.transfers.aht += 1.5; // Standard transfer AHT
                }
                else if (caseData.type === 'Paragon') {
                    metrics.paragon.total++;
                    metrics.paragon.totalAHT += parseFloat(caseData.aht) || 0;

                    // Check if HSI queue
                    if (caseData.queue && caseData.queue.toLowerCase().includes('hsi')) {
                        metrics.paragon.hsi.count++;
                        metrics.paragon.hsi.aht += parseFloat(caseData.aht) || 0;
                    } else {
                        metrics.paragon.regular.count++;
                        metrics.paragon.regular.aht += parseFloat(caseData.aht) || 0;
                    }
                }
                else if (caseData.type === 'Photon') {
                    metrics.photon.total++;
                    metrics.photon.totalAHT += parseFloat(caseData.aht) || 0;

                    const category = caseData.queue.toLowerCase().includes('sme') ? 'sme' : 'regular';
                    const uowType = caseData.status || 'Unknown';

                    // Initialize UoW type if not exists
                    if (!metrics.photon[category][uowType]) {
                        metrics.photon[category][uowType] = { count: 0, aht: 0 };
                    }

                    metrics.photon[category][uowType].count++;
                    metrics.photon[category][uowType].aht += parseFloat(caseData.aht) || 0;
                }
            });

            console.log('Calculated Metrics:', {
                selectedMonth,
                metrics,
                totalCases: metrics.paragon.total + metrics.photon.total + metrics.transfers.total
            });

            return metrics;
        };

        // Setup tab switching
        const tabs = window.dashboardWindow.document.querySelectorAll('.nav-tabs button');
        tabs.forEach((tab, index) => {
            tab.addEventListener('click', () => {
                // Remove active class from all tabs
                tabs.forEach(t => t.classList.remove('active'));
                // Add active class to clicked tab
                tab.classList.add('active');

                const dashboardContent = window.dashboardWindow.document.querySelector('.dashboard-content');
                const analyticsContent = window.dashboardWindow.document.querySelector('.analytics-content');
                const caseManagementContent = window.dashboardWindow.document.querySelector('.case-table-container');
                const performanceSummaryContent = window.dashboardWindow.document.querySelector('.performance-summary');
                const scorecardContent = window.dashboardWindow.document.querySelector('.scorecard-content');
                const calendarContent = window.dashboardWindow.document.querySelector('.calendar-content');

                // Hide all contents first
                [dashboardContent, analyticsContent, caseManagementContent,
                 performanceSummaryContent, scorecardContent, calendarContent].forEach(content => {
                    if (content) content.style.display = 'none';
                });
                // Show selected content
                switch(index) {
                    case 0: // Dashboard
                        if (dashboardContent) {
                            dashboardContent.style.display = 'block';
                            window.dashboardWindow.updateDashboardMetrics();
                        }

                        break;

                    case 1: // Case Management
                        if (!caseManagementContent) {
                            const div = window.dashboardWindow.document.createElement('div');
                            div.innerHTML = CASE_MANAGEMENT_HTML;
                            window.dashboardWindow.document.body.appendChild(div);
                            caseManagementContent = window.dashboardWindow.document.querySelector('.case-table-container');
                            // Add click handler for export button
                            const exportBtn = window.dashboardWindow.document.querySelector('.export-btn');
                            if (exportBtn) {
                                exportBtn.addEventListener('click', () => window.dashboardWindow.exportCaseData());
                            }

                            // Initialize filters and date selector
                            window.dashboardWindow.initializeFilterOptions();
                            window.dashboardWindow.initializeDateSelector();
                        }
                        if (caseManagementContent) {
                            caseManagementContent.style.display = 'block';
                            // Force immediate data refresh when switching to this tab
                            window.dashboardWindow.updateCaseManagement();

                            // Add a small delay to ensure data is properly loaded
                            setTimeout(() => {
                                window.dashboardWindow.updateCaseManagement();
                            }, 100);
                        }
                        break;

                    case 2: // Analytics
                        if (analyticsContent) {
                            analyticsContent.style.display = 'block';
                            // Initialize analytics date picker if not already initialized
                            if (!window.dashboardWindow.analyticsInitialized) {
                                const analyticsDatePicker = window.dashboardWindow.document.getElementById('analyticsDatePicker');
                                if (analyticsDatePicker) {
                                    analyticsDatePicker.addEventListener('change', (e) => {
                                        window.dashboardWindow.updateCharts(e.target.value);
                                    });
                                }
                                window.dashboardWindow.analyticsInitialized = true;
                            }
                            // Initialize or update charts
                            if (!window.dashboardWindow.charts) {
                                window.dashboardWindow.initializeCharts();
                            }
                            window.dashboardWindow.updateCharts();
                        }
                        break;
                    case 3: // Performance Summary
                        if (performanceSummaryContent) {
                            performanceSummaryContent.style.display = 'block';

                            if (!window.dashboardWindow.performanceCharts) {
                                window.dashboardWindow.initializePerformanceCharts();
                            }

                            // Only set up event listeners once
                            if (!window.dashboardWindow.periodButtonsInitialized) {
                                const buttons = performanceSummaryContent.querySelectorAll('.period-btn');

                                buttons.forEach(button => {
                                    button.addEventListener('click', function() {
                                        // Stop any existing interval
                                        if (window.performanceSummaryInterval) {
                                            clearInterval(window.performanceSummaryInterval);
                                            window.performanceSummaryInterval = null;
                                        }

                                        // Update state
                                        DASHBOARD_STATE.period = this.dataset.period;

                                        // Update UI
                                        buttons.forEach(btn => btn.classList.remove('active'));
                                        this.classList.add('active');

                                        // Update content
                                        window.dashboardWindow.updatePerformanceSummary();
                                    });
                                });

                                window.dashboardWindow.periodButtonsInitialized = true;
                            }

                            // Initial update
                            window.dashboardWindow.updatePerformanceSummary();

                            // Set up new interval
                            if (!window.performanceSummaryInterval) {
                                window.performanceSummaryInterval = setInterval(() => {
                                    if (window.dashboardWindow && !window.dashboardWindow.closed) {
                                        window.dashboardWindow.updatePerformanceSummary();
                                    } else {
                                        clearInterval(window.performanceSummaryInterval);
                                        window.performanceSummaryInterval = null;
                                    }
                                }, 5000);
                            }
                        }
                        break;
                    case 4: // Scorecard
                        if (scorecardContent) {
                            scorecardContent.style.display = 'block';
                            if (!window.dashboardWindow.scorecardInitialized) {
                                // We'll add initialization here later
                                window.dashboardWindow.initializeScorecard();
                                window.dashboardWindow.initializeScorecardCharts(); // Add this line
                            }
                            window.dashboardWindow.updateScorecard();
                        }
                        break;
                    case 5: // Calendar (new)
                        if (calendarContent) {
                            calendarContent.style.display = 'block';
                            if (!window.dashboardWindow.calendarInstance) {
                                window.dashboardWindow.calendarInstance = new window.dashboardWindow.Calendar();
                            }
                        }
                        break;
                }
            });
        });

        // Initial refresh
        window.dashboardWindow.refreshDashboard();

        // Auto refresh every 30 seconds
        setInterval(() => {
            if (window.dashboardWindow && !window.dashboardWindow.closed) {
                window.dashboardWindow.refreshDashboard();
            }
        }, 30000);

                    data: {

                            data: [],

                            stack: 'stack1'

                    },

        };


        // Setup metrics update function
        window.dashboardWindow.updateDashboardMetrics = function() {
            const cases = CaseSystem.cases;
            const today = new Date();
            today.setHours(0, 0, 0, 0);

            const TRANSFER_AHT = 1.5; // Fixed AHT for transfers

            const metrics = {
                total: { paragon: 0, photon: 0, transfers: 0 },
                today: { paragon: 0, photon: 0, transfers: 0 },
                totalAHT: { paragon: 0, photon: 0, transfers: 0 },
                todayAHT: { paragon: 0, photon: 0, transfers: 0 },
                asinAdjustments: { total: 0, today: 0 }  // Add ASIN tracking
            };

            Object.values(cases).forEach(caseData => {
                const caseDate = new Date(caseData.date);
                caseDate.setHours(0, 0, 0, 0);
                const isToday = caseDate.getTime() === today.getTime();

                let type;
                let aht;

                // Base AHT calculation
                if (caseData.isTransfer || caseData.type === 'Transfer') {
                    type = 'transfers';
                    aht = TRANSFER_AHT;
                } else {
                    type = caseData.type.toLowerCase();
                    aht = parseFloat(caseData.aht) || 0; // Keep original AHT
                }

                // Update metrics differently for counts vs AHT
                if (isToday) {
                    // AHT calculations should include all cases
                    metrics.todayAHT[type] += aht;

                    // Case counts should respect Work-in-Progress for Paragon
                    if (type === 'paragon') {
                        if (caseData.status === 'Work-in-Progress') {
                            metrics.today[type]++;
                        }
                    } else {
                        metrics.today[type]++;
                    }

                    // ASIN adjustments
                    if (caseData.asinCount > 3 && !caseData.isTransfer) {
                        const asinAdjustment = ((caseData.asinCount - 3) * 30) / 60;
                        metrics.asinAdjustments.today += asinAdjustment;
                    }
                }

                // Total metrics should include all cases
                metrics.total[type]++;
                metrics.totalAHT[type] += aht;

                if (caseData.asinCount > 3 && !caseData.isTransfer) {
                    const asinAdjustment = ((caseData.asinCount - 3) * 30) / 60;
                    metrics.asinAdjustments.total += asinAdjustment;
                }
            });
            // Update dashboard elements
            const doc = this.document;

            // Update Total Cases
            const totalCases = metrics.total.paragon + metrics.total.photon + metrics.total.transfers;
            doc.getElementById('totalCases').textContent = totalCases;
            doc.getElementById('totalCasesBreakdown').textContent =
                `Paragon: ${metrics.total.paragon} || Photon: ${metrics.total.photon} || Transfers: ${metrics.total.transfers}`;

            // Calculate total cases for today without validation
            const totalTodayCases = Object.values(cases).filter(caseData => {
                const caseDate = new Date(caseData.date);
                return caseDate.toDateString() === today.toDateString();
            }).length;

            // Update the main Today's Cases count to show total
            const todayCasesElement = doc.getElementById('todayCases');
            todayCasesElement.textContent = totalTodayCases;  // Show total count (69)

            // Show breakdown including active cases
            doc.getElementById('todayCasesBreakdown').innerHTML = `
    Active (Work-in-Progress): ${metrics.today.paragon}
    <span title="Only Work-in-Progress cases" style="color: #4caf50; font-size: 12px;">
        (validated)
    </span>
    || Photon: ${metrics.today.photon}
    || Transfers: ${metrics.today.transfers}
`;

            todayCasesElement.title = `Total Cases: ${totalTodayCases}\nActive Cases: ${metrics.today.paragon}`;



            // Update Today's Transfers specifically
            const todayTransfersElement = doc.getElementById('todayTransfers');
            if (todayTransfersElement) {
                todayTransfersElement.textContent = metrics.today.transfers;
                console.log('Updated transfer count:', metrics.today.transfers);
            }

            // Update transfers breakdown with correct AHT calculation
            const transfersBreakdown = doc.getElementById('transfersBreakdown');
            if (transfersBreakdown) {
                const totalTransferAHT = metrics.today.transfers * TRANSFER_AHT;
                transfersBreakdown.textContent =
                    `Total: ${metrics.today.transfers} || AHT: ${totalTransferAHT.toFixed(1)}m`;
                console.log('Updated transfer breakdown:', transfersBreakdown.textContent);
            }

            // Update transfer card styling
            const transferCard = doc.querySelector('.transfer-card');
            if (transferCard && todayTransfersElement) {
                if (metrics.today.transfers > 0) {
                    transferCard.style.borderLeft = '4px solid #1976d2';
                    todayTransfersElement.style.color = '#1976d2';
                } else {
                    transferCard.style.borderLeft = '4px solid #ddd';
                    todayTransfersElement.style.color = 'inherit';
                }
            }

            // Calculate total AHT including ASIN adjustments
            const todayTotalAHT = metrics.todayAHT.paragon +
                  metrics.todayAHT.photon +
                  metrics.todayAHT.transfers +
                  metrics.asinAdjustments.today;
            const targetMinutes = 480; // 8 hours in minutes
            AHTTracker.updateAHTDisplay(todayTotalAHT);

            // Get total productive time in minutes (including both current and accumulated)
            const totalProductiveSeconds = CaseSystem.auxTotals.dailyTotals.productive +
                  (CaseSystem.getAuxCategory(CaseSystem.auxTotals.lastStatus) === 'productive' ?
                   CaseSystem.auxTotals.productive : 0);

            const productiveTimeInMinutes = Math.max(Math.floor(totalProductiveSeconds / 60), 1);

            // Update Today's AHT display
            doc.getElementById('todayAHT').textContent = `${todayTotalAHT.toFixed(1)}/${targetMinutes} mins`;
            // Enhanced AHT breakdown with ASIN adjustments
            const asinAdjustedCases = Object.values(cases)
            .filter(c => c.asinCount > 3 && new Date(c.date).toDateString() === today.toDateString())
            .length;

            doc.getElementById('todayAHTBreakdown').textContent =
                `Paragon: ${metrics.todayAHT.paragon} || ` +
                `Photon: ${metrics.todayAHT.photon} || ` +
                `Transfers: ${(metrics.today.transfers * TRANSFER_AHT).toFixed(1)}` +
                (metrics.asinAdjustments.today > 0 ?
                 ` || ASIN Adj: +${metrics.asinAdjustments.today.toFixed(1)}m (${asinAdjustedCases} cases)` :
                 '');
            // Calculate High ASIN metrics
            const highAsinCases = Object.values(cases)
            .filter(c => {
                const caseDate = new Date(c.date);
                return caseDate.toDateString() === today.toDateString() &&
                    c.asinCount > 3;
            });

            const highAsinMetrics = {
                count: highAsinCases.length,
                totalAddonTime: highAsinCases.reduce((total, c) => {
                    return total + ((c.asinCount - 3) * 30) / 60;
                }, 0)
            };

            // Update High ASIN Cases card
            const highAsinElement = doc.getElementById('highAsinCount');
            if (highAsinElement) {
                const countElement = highAsinElement.querySelector('.count');
                const timeElement = highAsinElement.querySelector('.time');

                // Update with animation
                if (countElement) {
                    const oldCount = parseInt(countElement.textContent) || 0;
                    countElement.textContent = highAsinMetrics.count;
                    if (oldCount !== highAsinMetrics.count) {
                        countElement.classList.add('value-update');
                        setTimeout(() => countElement.classList.remove('value-update'), 300);
                    }
                }

                if (timeElement) {
                    const oldTime = parseFloat(timeElement.textContent) || 0;
                    timeElement.textContent = `+${highAsinMetrics.totalAddonTime.toFixed(1)}m`;
                    if (oldTime !== highAsinMetrics.totalAddonTime) {
                        timeElement.classList.add('value-update');
                        setTimeout(() => timeElement.classList.remove('value-update'), 300);
                    }
                }
            }

            // Optional: Add breakdown
            const breakdownElement = doc.getElementById('highAsinBreakdown');
            if (breakdownElement && highAsinMetrics.count > 0) {
                // Group cases by ASIN count
                const asinGroups = highAsinCases.reduce((acc, c) => {
                    acc[c.asinCount] = (acc[c.asinCount] || 0) + 1;
                    return acc;
                }, {});

                breakdownElement.textContent = Object.entries(asinGroups)
                    .map(([asinCount, cases]) => `${asinCount} ASINs: ${cases} cases`)
                    .join(' | ');
            }

            // Add ASIN adjustment indicator if applicable
            const ahtElement = doc.getElementById('todayAHT');
            if (metrics.asinAdjustments.today > 0) {
                if (!doc.getElementById('asin-indicator')) {
                    const indicator = document.createElement('div');
                    indicator.id = 'asin-indicator';
                    indicator.className = 'asin-adjustment-indicator';
                    indicator.innerHTML = `
                <span class="material-icons">add_circle</span>
                Includes ${metrics.asinAdjustments.today.toFixed(1)}m ASIN adjustment
            `;
                    ahtElement.parentNode.insertBefore(indicator, ahtElement.nextSibling);
                }
            }

            // Update Total AHT
            const totalAHT = metrics.totalAHT.paragon + metrics.totalAHT.photon + (metrics.total.transfers * TRANSFER_AHT);
            doc.getElementById('totalAHT').textContent = `${totalAHT.toFixed(1)} mins`;
            doc.getElementById('totalAHTBreakdown').textContent =
                `Paragon: ${metrics.totalAHT.paragon} || ` +
                `Photon: ${metrics.totalAHT.photon} || ` +
                `Transfers: ${(metrics.total.transfers * TRANSFER_AHT).toFixed(1)}` +
                (metrics.asinAdjustments.total > 0 ?
                 ` || Total ASIN Adj: +${metrics.asinAdjustments.total.toFixed(1)}m` :
                 '');

            // Add styles for ASIN indicator
            if (!doc.getElementById('asin-indicator-styles')) {
                const style = doc.createElement('style');
                style.id = 'asin-indicator-styles';
                style.textContent = `
            .asin-adjustment-indicator {
                font-size: 12px;
                color: #ff9900;
                display: flex;
                align-items: center;
                gap: 4px;
                margin-top: 4px;
                padding: 4px 8px;
                background: rgba(255, 153, 0, 0.1);
                border-radius: 4px;
                animation: fadeIn 0.3s ease;
            }
            .asin-adjustment-indicator .material-icons {
                font-size: 14px;
            }
            @keyframes fadeIn {
                from { opacity: 0; transform: translateY(-4px); }
                to { opacity: 1; transform: translateY(0); }
            }
        `;
                doc.head.appendChild(style);
            }
            let efficiency = CaseSystem.calculateEfficiency(todayTotalAHT, productiveTimeInMinutes);

            // Update Efficiency Display
            const efficiencyElement = doc.getElementById('efficiency');
            const efficiencyBreakdown = doc.getElementById('efficiencyBreakdown');

            if (efficiencyElement) {
                efficiencyElement.textContent = `${efficiency}%`;
                efficiencyElement.style.color =
                    efficiency > 150 ? '#d13212' :  // Red for very high values
                efficiency > 100 ? '#ff9900' :  // Orange for over 100%
                efficiency >= 90 ? '#4caf50' :  // Green for good efficiency
                '#ff9900';  // Orange for lower efficiency
            }

            if (efficiencyBreakdown) {
                efficiencyBreakdown.textContent =
                    `AHT: ${todayTotalAHT.toFixed(1)}m / Productive: ${productiveTimeInMinutes}m`;
            }
            QuickStats.update();
            this.updateScheduleDisplay();  // Add this line
            this.updateOTDisplay();  // Add this line

            // Update Quick Stats if initialized
            if (typeof QuickStats !== 'undefined') {
                QuickStats.updateStats();
            }

            // Update AHT Tracker if initialized
            if (typeof AHTTracker !== 'undefined') {
                AHTTracker.updateAHTDisplay(todayTotalAHT);
            }


            // Log debugging information
            console.log('Metrics Update:', {
                today: metrics.today,
                todayAHT: metrics.todayAHT,
                transfers: metrics.today.transfers,
                transferAHT: metrics.today.transfers * TRANSFER_AHT,
                efficiency: efficiency,
                productiveTime: productiveTimeInMinutes,
                asinAdjustments: {
                    today: metrics.asinAdjustments.today,
                    total: metrics.asinAdjustments.total,
                    adjustedCases: asinAdjustedCases
                }
            });
            // Log debugging information
            console.log('Efficiency Calculation:', {
                todayTotalAHT,
                productiveTimeInMinutes,
                totalProductiveSeconds,
                efficiency,
                auxTotals: CaseSystem.auxTotals
            });
            console.log('Final metrics:', metrics);
        };


        window.dashboardWindow.initializeCharts = function() {
            const ctx = {
                efficiency: this.document.getElementById('dailyProductivityChart')?.getContext('2d'),
                aht: this.document.getElementById('ahtTrendChart')?.getContext('2d'),
                queue: this.document.getElementById('queueDistributionChart')?.getContext('2d'),
                caseType: this.document.getElementById('caseTypeChart')?.getContext('2d'),
                productiveTime: this.document.getElementById('productiveTimeChart')?.getContext('2d'),
                otAnalysis:this.document.getElementById('otAnalysisChart')?.getContext('2d')
            };

            if (!ctx.efficiency || !ctx.aht || !ctx.queue || !ctx.caseType ||
                !ctx.productiveTime){
                console.error('Missing chart contexts');
                return;
            }

            // Common chart configurations
            const commonOptions = {
                responsive: true,
                maintainAspectRatio: false,
                responsive: true,
                layout: {
                    padding: {
                        top: 20,
                        right: 20,
                        bottom: 20,
                        left: 20
                    }
                },
                animation: {
                    duration: 2000,
                    easing: 'easeInOutQuart'
                },
                plugins: {
                    legend: {
                        position: 'right',
                        labels: {
                            usePointStyle: true,
                            padding: 20,
                            font: {
                                family: "'Arial', sans-serif",
                                size: 12,
                                weight: 500
                            },
                            generateLabels: (chart) => {
                                const datasets = chart.data.datasets;
                                return datasets.map(dataset => ({
                                    text: dataset.label,
                                    fillStyle: dataset.backgroundColor,
                                    strokeStyle: dataset.borderColor || dataset.backgroundColor,
                                    lineWidth: 2,
                                    hidden: !chart.isDatasetVisible(datasets.indexOf(dataset)),
                                    index: datasets.indexOf(dataset)
                                }));
                            }
                        },
                        onClick: (e, legendItem, legend) => {
                            const index = legendItem.index;
                            const chart = legend.chart;
                            const isHidden = chart.isDatasetVisible(index);

                            chart.setDatasetVisibility(index, !isHidden);
                            chart.update();
                        }
                    },
                    tooltip: {
                        backgroundColor: 'rgba(35, 47, 62, 0.95)',
                        titleFont: {
                            size: 14,
                            weight: 'bold'
                        },
                        bodyFont: {
                            size: 13
                        },
                        padding: 12,
                        cornerRadius: 8,
                        usePointStyle: true,
                        animation: {
                            duration: 150
                        }
                    }
                }
            };

            this.charts = {
                // Efficiency Chart
                efficiency: new Chart(ctx.efficiency, {
                    type: 'line',
                    data: {
                        labels: [],
                        datasets: [{
                            label: 'Efficiency',
                            data: [],
                            borderColor: '#ff9900',
                            backgroundColor: (context) => {
                                const gradient = context.chart.ctx.createLinearGradient(0, 0, 0, 400);
                                gradient.addColorStop(0, 'rgba(255, 153, 0, 0.2)');
                                gradient.addColorStop(1, 'rgba(255, 153, 0, 0)');
                                return gradient;
                            },
                            borderWidth: 2,
                            fill: true,
                            tension: 0.4,
                            pointBackgroundColor: '#ffffff',
                            pointBorderColor: '#ff9900',
                            pointBorderWidth: 2,
                            pointRadius: 4,
                            pointHoverRadius: 6
                        }, {
                            label: 'Target',
                            data: [], // Will be filled with 100%
                            borderColor: 'rgba(35, 47, 62, 0.2)',
                            borderDash: [5, 5],
                            borderWidth: 1,
                            pointRadius: 0,
                            fill: false
                        }]
                    },
                    options: {
                        ...commonOptions,
                        scales: {
                            y: {
                                beginAtZero: true,
                                grid: {
                                    drawBorder: false,
                                    color: 'rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.05)'
                                },
                                ticks: {
                                    callback: value => `${value}%`,
                                    font: {
                                        size: 11
                                    }
                                }
                            },
                            x: {
                                grid: {
                                    display: false
                                },
                                ticks: {
                                    font: {
                                        size: 11
                                    }
                                }
                            }
                        },
                        plugins: {
                            ...commonOptions.plugins,
                            tooltip: {
                                ...commonOptions.plugins.tooltip,
                                callbacks: {
                                    label: (context) => {
                                        const value = context.raw;
                                        const efficiency = value.toFixed(1);
                                        const variance = (value - 100).toFixed(1);
                                        const status = value >= 100 ? '✅' : '⚠️';

                                        return [
                                            `${status} Efficiency: ${efficiency}%`,
                                            `Variance from target: ${variance}%`
                                        ];
                                    }
                                }
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }),
                // Case Distribution Chart
                caseCount: new Chart(ctx.aht, {
                    type: 'bar',
                    data: {
                        labels: [],
                        datasets: [{
                            label: 'Transfers',
                            data: [],
                            backgroundColor: 'rgba(25, 118, 210, 0.8)',
                            hoverBackgroundColor: 'rgba(25, 118, 210, 1)',
                            borderRadius: 6,
                            borderWidth: 2,
                            borderColor: 'rgba(25, 118, 210, 0.9)'
                        }, {
                            label: 'Photon',
                            data: [],
                            backgroundColor: 'rgba(255, 153, 0, 0.8)',
                            hoverBackgroundColor: 'rgba(255, 153, 0, 1)',

                            borderWidth: 2,

                        plugins: {

                                        const value = context.parsed || 0;
                                        const total = context.dataset.data.reduce((a, b) => a + b, 0);
                                        const percentage = ((value / total) * 100).toFixed(1);

                                        return value + 'h';
                                    }
                                }
                            }
                        },
                        plugins: {
                            legend: {
                                position: 'top',
                                align: 'end'
                            },
                            tooltip: {
                                mode: 'index',

                                callbacks: {
                                    title: function(tooltipItems) {
                                        return tooltipItems[0].label;
                                    },
                                    label: function(context) {
                                        const hours = Math.floor(context.raw);
                                        const minutes = Math.round((context.raw - hours) * 60);
                                        return `${context.dataset.label}: ${hours}h ${minutes}m`;
                                    },
                                    footer: function(tooltipItems) {
                                        const total = tooltipItems.reduce((sum, ti) => sum + ti.raw, 0);
                                        const hours = Math.floor(total);
                                        const minutes = Math.round((total - hours) * 60);
                                        return `Total: ${hours}h ${minutes}m`;
                                    }
                                }
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }),
                otAnalysis: new Chart(ctx.otAnalysis , {

                    data: {

                                        const minutes = Math.round((context.raw % 1) * 60);
