                                    text: 'Hours'
                                },
                                ticks: {
                                    callback: function(value) {
                                        return `${value}h`;
                                    }
                                }
                            }
                        }
                    }
                })
            };

            // Add hover animation effects
            Object.values(this.charts).forEach(chart => {
                chart.options.onHover = (event, elements) => {
                    if (elements && elements.length) {
                        event.native.target.style.cursor = 'pointer';
                    } else {
                        event.native.target.style.cursor = 'default';
                    }
                };
            });
        };

        window.dashboardWindow.updateProductiveTimeAnalytics = function(selectedDate = null) {
            const dailyData = {};
            let totalProductiveHours = 0;
            let totalNonProductiveHours = 0;
            let totalOfflineHours = 0;

            const today = new Date().toLocaleDateString();

            if (selectedDate) {
                // Single date view
                const dateStr = new Date(selectedDate).toLocaleDateString();

                // Get stored AUX data for the selected date
                const storedData = GM_getValue(`auxData_${dateStr}`);
                if (storedData) {
                    const auxData = JSON.parse(storedData);
                    if (dateStr === today) {
                        // For today, include current state
                        dailyData[dateStr] = {
                            productive: (auxData.productive +
                                         (CaseSystem.getAuxCategory(CaseSystem.auxState.currentStatus) === 'productive' ?
                                          CaseSystem.auxTotals.productive : 0)) / 3600,
                            nonProductive: (auxData.nonProductive +
                                            (CaseSystem.getAuxCategory(CaseSystem.auxState.currentStatus) === 'nonProductive' ?
                                             CaseSystem.auxTotals.nonProductive : 0)) / 3600,
                            offline: (auxData.offline +
                                      (CaseSystem.getAuxCategory(CaseSystem.auxState.currentStatus) === 'offline' ?
                                       CaseSystem.auxTotals.offline : 0)) / 3600
                        };
                    } else {
                        // For historical dates, use stored data only
                        dailyData[dateStr] = {
                            productive: auxData.productive / 3600,
                            nonProductive: auxData.nonProductive / 3600,
                            offline: auxData.offline / 3600
                        };
                    }
                }

                // Calculate totals for single date
                totalProductiveHours = dailyData[dateStr]?.productive || 0;
                totalNonProductiveHours = dailyData[dateStr]?.nonProductive || 0;
                totalOfflineHours = dailyData[dateStr]?.offline || 0;

                // Debug logging
                console.log('Single Date AUX Data:', {
                    date: dateStr,
                    stored: storedData ? JSON.parse(storedData) : null,
                    current: CaseSystem.auxTotals,
                    calculated: dailyData[dateStr]
                });
            } else {
                // Original 30-day view logic
                const days = 30;
                const endDate = new Date();
                const startDate = new Date();
                startDate.setDate(endDate.getDate() - days);

                // Initialize dates for 30-day view
                for (let d = new Date(startDate); d <= endDate; d.setDate(d.getDate() + 1)) {
                    const dateStr = d.toLocaleDateString();
                    dailyData[dateStr] = {
                        productive: 0,
                        nonProductive: 0,
                        offline: 0
                    };
                }

                // Get current day's data
                const currentDayData = {
                    productive: (CaseSystem.auxTotals.dailyTotals.productive +
                                 (CaseSystem.getAuxCategory(CaseSystem.auxState.currentStatus) === 'productive' ?
                                  CaseSystem.auxTotals.productive : 0)) / 3600,
                    nonProductive: (CaseSystem.auxTotals.dailyTotals.nonProductive +
                                    (CaseSystem.getAuxCategory(CaseSystem.auxState.currentStatus) === 'nonProductive' ?
                                     CaseSystem.auxTotals.nonProductive : 0)) / 3600,
                    offline: (CaseSystem.auxTotals.dailyTotals.offline +
                              (CaseSystem.getAuxCategory(CaseSystem.auxState.currentStatus) === 'offline' ?
                               CaseSystem.auxTotals.offline : 0)) / 3600
                };

                // Process all dates
                Object.keys(dailyData).forEach(dateStr => {
                    if (dateStr === today) {
                        dailyData[dateStr] = currentDayData;
                    } else {
                        const storedData = GM_getValue(`auxData_${dateStr}`);
                        if (storedData) {
                            const auxData = JSON.parse(storedData);
                            dailyData[dateStr] = {
                                productive: auxData.productive / 3600,
                                nonProductive: auxData.nonProductive / 3600,
                                offline: auxData.offline / 3600
                            };
                        }
                    }

                    // Accumulate totals
                    totalProductiveHours += dailyData[dateStr].productive;
                    totalNonProductiveHours += dailyData[dateStr].nonProductive;
                    totalOfflineHours += dailyData[dateStr].offline;
                });
            }

            // Update charts with the data
            const dates = Object.keys(dailyData);
            const formattedDates = dates.map(date =>
                                             new Date(date).toLocaleDateString('en-US', { month: 'short', day: 'numeric' })
                                            );

            // Update Productive Time Chart
            this.charts.productiveTime.data.labels = formattedDates;
            this.charts.productiveTime.data.datasets[0].data = dates.map(date =>
                                                                         Number((dailyData[date]?.productive || 0).toFixed(2))
                                                                        );
            this.charts.productiveTime.data.datasets[1].data = dates.map(date =>
                                                                         Number((dailyData[date]?.nonProductive || 0).toFixed(2))
                                                                        );
            this.charts.productiveTime.data.datasets[2].data = dates.map(date =>
                                                                         Number((dailyData[date]?.offline || 0).toFixed(2))
                                                                        );
            this.charts.productiveTime.update('active');



            // Update summary metrics with proper time calculations
            const days = selectedDate ? 1 : 30;
            const averageProductiveHours = totalProductiveHours / days;
            const totalTime = totalProductiveHours + totalNonProductiveHours + totalOfflineHours;
            const productivityRate = totalTime > 0 ? (totalProductiveHours / totalTime) * 100 : 0;

            // Update the summary display
            const timeSummaryElement = this.document.querySelector('.time-summary');
            if (timeSummaryElement) {
                timeSummaryElement.innerHTML = `
            <div class="time-metric">
                <div class="time-metric-value">
                    ${Math.floor(totalProductiveHours)}h ${Math.round((totalProductiveHours % 1) * 60)}m
                </div>
                <div class="time-metric-label">Total Productive Time</div>
            </div>
            <div class="time-metric">
                <div class="time-metric-value">${averageProductiveHours.toFixed(1)}h</div>
                <div class="time-metric-label">${selectedDate ? 'Productive Time' : 'Avg. Daily Productive Time'}</div>
            </div>
            <div class="time-metric">
                <div class="time-metric-value">${Math.round(productivityRate)}%</div>
                <div class="time-metric-label">Productivity Rate</div>
            </div>
        `;
            }

            // Debug logging
            console.log('AUX Time Analytics Update:', {
                selectedDate,
                dailyData,
                totals: {
                    productive: totalProductiveHours,
                    nonProductive: totalNonProductiveHours,
                    offline: totalOfflineHours
                }
            });
        };

        window.dashboardWindow.updateCharts = function(selectedDate = null) {
            const cases = CaseSystem.cases;
            if (!cases || !this.charts) return;

            const dailyEfficiency = {};
            const dailyCaseCounts = {};
            const queueCounts = {};
            const typeCounts = {
                Paragon: 0,
                Photon: 0,
                Transfer: 0
            };

            // Get OT metrics
            const otMetrics = this.calculateOTMetrics();

            // Initialize arrays for 30-day window
            const endDate = new Date();
            const startDate = new Date();
            startDate.setDate(endDate.getDate() - 30);

            const dates = [];
            const regularOT = [];
            const weekoffOT = [];

            const today = new Date().toLocaleDateString();
            if (selectedDate) {
                // Single date view
                const dateStr = new Date(selectedDate).toLocaleDateString();

                // Initialize for selected date
                dailyEfficiency[dateStr] = {
                    totalAHT: 0,
                    productiveTime: dateStr === today ?
                    Math.max(Math.floor((CaseSystem.auxTotals.dailyTotals.productive +
                                         CaseSystem.auxTotals.productive) / 60), 1) : 480
                };

                dailyCaseCounts[dateStr] = {
                    paragon: 0,
                    photon: 0,
                    transfers: 0
                };

                // Filter cases for selected date
                const filteredCases = Object.values(cases).filter(caseData => {
                    const caseDate = new Date(caseData.date).toLocaleDateString();
                    return caseDate === dateStr;
                });

                // Process filtered cases
                filteredCases.forEach(caseData => {
                    const aht = parseFloat(caseData.aht) || 0;
                    let type = caseData.isTransfer ? 'Transfer' : caseData.type;
                    typeCounts[type] = (typeCounts[type] || 0) + 1;

                    if (caseData.isTransfer) {
                        dailyCaseCounts[dateStr].transfers++;
                    } else if (caseData.type === 'Photon') {
                        dailyCaseCounts[dateStr].photon++;
                    } else if (caseData.type === 'Paragon') {
                        dailyCaseCounts[dateStr].paragon++;
                    }

                    dailyEfficiency[dateStr].totalAHT += aht;

                    if (!caseData.isTransfer) {
                        const queue = caseData.queue || 'Unknown';
                        queueCounts[queue] = (queueCounts[queue] || 0) + 1;
                    }
                });

                // Update analytics count display
                const analyticsCount = this.document.getElementById('analyticsSpecificCount');
                if (analyticsCount) {
                    analyticsCount.textContent = `${filteredCases.length} cases on ${dateStr}`;
                }

                // Update display text
                const analyticsDisplayDate = this.document.getElementById('analyticsDisplayDate');
                if (analyticsDisplayDate) {
                    analyticsDisplayDate.textContent = dateStr === today ?
                        "Today's Analytics" :
                    new Date(selectedDate).toLocaleDateString();
                }
            } else {
                // 30-day view
                for(let i = 30; i >= 0; i--) {
                    const date = new Date();
                    date.setDate(date.getDate() - i);
                    const dateStr = date.toLocaleDateString();

                    const productiveTime = dateStr === today ?
                          Math.max(Math.floor((CaseSystem.auxTotals.dailyTotals.productive +
                                               CaseSystem.auxTotals.productive) / 60), 1) : 480;

                    dailyEfficiency[dateStr] = {
                        totalAHT: 0,
                        productiveTime: productiveTime
                    };

                    dailyCaseCounts[dateStr] = {
                        paragon: 0,
                        photon: 0,
                        transfers: 0
                    };
                }

                // Process all cases
                Object.values(cases).forEach(caseData => {
                    const date = new Date(caseData.date).toLocaleDateString();
                    const aht = parseFloat(caseData.aht) || 0;

                    let type = caseData.isTransfer ? 'Transfer' : caseData.type;
                    typeCounts[type] = (typeCounts[type] || 0) + 1;

                    if (dailyCaseCounts[date]) {
                        if (caseData.isTransfer) {
                            dailyCaseCounts[date].transfers++;
                        } else if (caseData.type === 'Photon') {
                            dailyCaseCounts[date].photon++;
                        } else if (caseData.type === 'Paragon') {
                            dailyCaseCounts[date].paragon++;
                        }
                    }

                    if (dailyEfficiency[date]) {
                        dailyEfficiency[date].totalAHT += aht;
                    }

                    if (!caseData.isTransfer) {
                        const queue = caseData.queue || 'Unknown';
                        queueCounts[queue] = (queueCounts[queue] || 0) + 1;
                    }
                });

                // Reset analytics display for 30-day view
                const analyticsCount = this.document.getElementById('analyticsSpecificCount');
                if (analyticsCount) {
                    const totalCases = Object.values(dailyCaseCounts).reduce((sum, day) =>
                                                                             sum + day.paragon + day.photon + day.transfers, 0);
                    analyticsCount.textContent = `${totalCases} cases in last 30 days`;
                }

                const analyticsDisplayDate = this.document.getElementById('analyticsDisplayDate');
                if (analyticsDisplayDate) {
                    analyticsDisplayDate.textContent = "Last 30 Days";
                }
            }
            // Process OT data for 30-day window
            for(let d = new Date(startDate); d <= endDate; d.setDate(d.getDate() + 1)) {
                const dateStr = d.toLocaleDateString();

                // Format date for display like other charts
                const displayDate = d.toLocaleDateString('en-US', {
                    month: 'short',
                    day: 'numeric'
                });
                dates.push(displayDate);

                // Find OT data for this date
                const dayData = otMetrics.details.find(detail => detail.date === dateStr);
                if (dayData) {
                    if (dayData.isWeekoff) {
                        weekoffOT.push(dayData.total);
                        regularOT.push(0);
                    } else {
                        regularOT.push(dayData.total);
                        weekoffOT.push(0);
                    }
                } else {
                    regularOT.push(0);
                    weekoffOT.push(0);
                }
            }

            // Calculate efficiency data
            const efficiencyData = Object.entries(dailyEfficiency).map(([date, data]) => {
                const efficiency = (data.productiveTime > 0) ?
                      Math.round((data.totalAHT / data.productiveTime) * 100 * 10) / 10 : 0;

                if (date === today) {
                    console.log('Today\'s Efficiency Calculation:', {
                        date: date,
                        totalAHT: data.totalAHT,
                        productiveTime: data.productiveTime,
                        efficiency: efficiency,
                        auxTotals: CaseSystem.auxTotals
                    });
                }

                return {
                    date: date,
                    efficiency: efficiency
                };
            });
            // 1. Efficiency Chart
            this.charts.efficiency.data.labels = efficiencyData.map(d => d.date);
            this.charts.efficiency.data.datasets[0].data = efficiencyData.map(d => d.efficiency);
            this.charts.efficiency.data.datasets[1].data = efficiencyData.map(() => 100);
            const maxEfficiency = Math.max(...efficiencyData.map(d => d.efficiency));
            this.charts.efficiency.options.scales.y.suggestedMax = Math.max(220, maxEfficiency + 20);
            this.charts.efficiency.update();

            // 2. Case Count Chart
            const caseDates = Object.keys(dailyCaseCounts);
            this.charts.caseCount.data.labels = caseDates;
            this.charts.caseCount.data.datasets[0].data = caseDates.map(date => dailyCaseCounts[date].transfers);
            this.charts.caseCount.data.datasets[1].data = caseDates.map(date => dailyCaseCounts[date].photon);
            this.charts.caseCount.data.datasets[2].data = caseDates.map(date => dailyCaseCounts[date].paragon);
            this.charts.caseCount.update();

            // 3. Queue Distribution Chart
            this.charts.queue.data.labels = Object.keys(queueCounts);
            this.charts.queue.data.datasets[0].data = Object.values(queueCounts);
            this.charts.queue.update();

            // 4. Case Type Chart
            this.charts.caseType.data.datasets[0].data = [
                typeCounts.Paragon || 0,
                typeCounts.Photon || 0,
                typeCounts.Transfer || 0
            ];
            this.charts.caseType.update();

            // 5. OT Analysis Chart
            // In updateCharts function, modify the OT Analysis Chart section:
            if (this.charts.otAnalysis) {
                // Calculate end date and start date for 30-day window
                const endDate = new Date();
                const startDate = new Date();
                startDate.setDate(endDate.getDate() - 30);

                // Get OT data for current month
                const currentMonthMetrics = this.calculateOTMetrics();

                // Get OT data for previous month if needed
                const previousMonthMetrics = startDate.getMonth() !== endDate.getMonth() ?
                      this.calculateOTMetrics(`${startDate.getFullYear()}-${String(startDate.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0')}`) :
                null;

                const dates = [];
                const regularOT = [];
                const weekoffOT = [];

                // Loop through 30-day window
                for(let d = new Date(startDate); d <= endDate; d.setDate(d.getDate() + 1)) {
                    const dateStr = d.toLocaleDateString();
                    const displayDate = d.toLocaleDateString('en-US', {
                        month: 'short',
                        day: 'numeric'
                    });
                    dates.push(displayDate);

                    // Check which month's data to use
                    const metricsToUse = d.getMonth() === endDate.getMonth() ?
                          currentMonthMetrics : previousMonthMetrics;

                    // Find this date's data
                    const dayData = metricsToUse?.details.find(detail => detail.date === dateStr);

                    if (dayData) {
                        if (dayData.isWeekoff) {
                            weekoffOT.push(dayData.total);
                            regularOT.push(0);
                        } else {
                            regularOT.push(dayData.total);
                            weekoffOT.push(0);
                        }
                    } else {
                        regularOT.push(0);
                        weekoffOT.push(0);
                    }
                }

                // Update chart with combined data
                this.charts.otAnalysis.data.labels = dates;
                this.charts.otAnalysis.data.datasets[0].data = regularOT;
                this.charts.otAnalysis.data.datasets[1].data = weekoffOT;
                this.charts.otAnalysis.update('none');

                // Debug logging
                console.log('OT Chart Data:', {
                    period: {
                        start: startDate.toLocaleDateString(),
                        end: endDate.toLocaleDateString()
                    },
                    currentMonthData: currentMonthMetrics,
                    previousMonthData: previousMonthMetrics,
                    chartData: {
                        dates,
                        regularOT,
                        weekoffOT
                    }
                });
            }
            // Update OT summary
            const formatTime = (hours) => {
                const h = Math.floor(hours);
                const m = Math.round((hours % 1) * 60);
                return `${h}h ${m}m`;
            };

            const otTotal = this.document.getElementById('otTotal');
            const regularOTSpan = this.document.getElementById('regularOT');
            const weekoffOTSpan = this.document.getElementById('weekoffOT');

            if (selectedDate) {
                const dateStr = new Date(selectedDate).toLocaleDateString();
                const dayData = otMetrics.details.find(detail => detail.date === dateStr) || { total: 0, isWeekoff: false };

                if (otTotal) otTotal.textContent = formatTime(dayData.total);
                if (regularOTSpan) regularOTSpan.textContent = formatTime(dayData.isWeekoff ? 0 : dayData.total);
                if (weekoffOTSpan) weekoffOTSpan.textContent = formatTime(dayData.isWeekoff ? dayData.total : 0);
            } else {
                if (otTotal) otTotal.textContent = formatTime(otMetrics.total);
                if (regularOTSpan) regularOTSpan.textContent = formatTime(otMetrics.regularDays);
                if (weekoffOTSpan) weekoffOTSpan.textContent = formatTime(otMetrics.weekoffDays);
            }

            // Update productive time analytics
            this.updateProductiveTimeAnalytics(selectedDate);

            // Log debug information
            console.log('Charts Updated:', {
                selectedDate: selectedDate,
                totalCases: typeCounts,
                efficiency: efficiencyData,
                queues: queueCounts,
                otMetrics: {
                    total: otMetrics.total,
                    regular: otMetrics.regularDays,
                    weekoff: otMetrics.weekoffDays,
                    dateRange: {
                        start: startDate.toLocaleDateString(),
                        end: endDate.toLocaleDateString()
                    }
                },
                otData: {
                    dates: dates,
                    regularOT: regularOT,
                    weekoffOT: weekoffOT
                }
            });
        };


        // Add these helper functions
        window.dashboardWindow.applyFilters = function() {
            this.updateCaseManagement();
        };

        window.dashboardWindow.clearFilters = function() {
            this.document.getElementById('dateFrom').value = '';
            this.document.getElementById('dateTo').value = '';
            this.document.getElementById('caseTypeFilter').value = '';
            this.updateCaseManagement();
        };

        // Update header with username
        const headerTitle = window.dashboardWindow.document.querySelector('.header h1');
        if (headerTitle) {
            headerTitle.textContent = `Productivity Tracker - ${UserSystem.currentUser}`;
        }

        // Setup logout button
        const logoutBtn = window.dashboardWindow.document.querySelector('.logout-btn');
        if (logoutBtn) {
            logoutBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
                UserSystem.logout();
                window.dashboardWindow.close();
            });
        }

        // Initial metrics update
        window.dashboardWindow.updateDashboardMetrics();
        // Add periodic sync check
        const syncInterval = setInterval(() => {
            if (window.dashboardWindow && !window.dashboardWindow.closed) {
                window.dashboardWindow.updateDashboardMetrics();
                window.dashboardWindow.updateCaseManagement();
            } else {
                clearInterval(syncInterval);
            }
        }, 2000);
    }

    // Add auto-refresh for dashboard
    const refreshInterval = setInterval(() => {
        if (window.dashboardWindow && !window.dashboardWindow.closed) {
            CaseSystem.processCaseUpdates();
        } else {
            clearInterval(refreshInterval);
        }
    }, 1000);

    // Update CaseSystem's updateDashboard method
    CaseSystem.updateDashboard = function() {
        if (window.dashboardWindow && !window.dashboardWindow.closed) {
            const activeTab = window.dashboardWindow.document.querySelector('.nav-tabs button.active');
            if (activeTab && activeTab.textContent.includes('Case Management')) {
                window.dashboardWindow.updateCaseManagement();
            } else {
                window.dashboardWindow.updateDashboardMetrics();
            }
        }
    }
    function initializePagination() {
        const itemsPerPage = parseInt(document.getElementById('rowsPerPage').value);
        const cases = Object.values(CaseSystem.cases);
        const totalPages = Math.ceil(cases.length / itemsPerPage);
        let currentPage = 1;

        function displayPage(pageNumber) {
            const start = (pageNumber - 1) * itemsPerPage;
            const end = start + itemsPerPage;
            const pageItems = cases
            .sort((a, b) => new Date(b.date) - new Date(a.date))
            .slice(start, end);

            const tbody = document.getElementById('caseTableBody');
            tbody.innerHTML = pageItems.map(caseData => `
            <tr class="${caseData.isTransfer ? 'transfer-row' : ''}">
                <td>${new Date(caseData.date).toLocaleDateString()}</td>
                <td>${caseData.id}</td>
                <td>${caseData.isTransfer ? 'Transfer' : caseData.type}</td>
                <td>${caseData.isTransfer ? 'N/A' : (caseData.queue || 'N/A')}</td>
                <td>${caseData.status || 'N/A'}</td>
                <td>${caseData.isTransfer ? 'N/A' : (caseData.reasonCode || 'N/A')}</td>
                <td>${caseData.aht || 0}</td>
            </tr>
        `).join('');

            updatePaginationControls(pageNumber, totalPages);
            updatePageInfo(start + 1, Math.min(end, cases.length), cases.length);
        }

        function updatePaginationControls(current, total) {
            const pageNumbers = document.getElementById('pageNumbers');
            pageNumbers.innerHTML = '';

            // Add page numbers with ellipsis
            let pages = [];
            if (total <= 7) {
                pages = Array.from({length: total}, (_, i) => i + 1);
            } else {
                if (current <= 3) {
                    pages = [1, 2, 3, 4, '...', total];
                } else if (current >= total - 2) {
                    pages = [1, '...', total - 3, total - 2, total - 1, total];
                } else {
                    pages = [1, '...', current - 1, current, current + 1, '...', total];
                }
            }

            pages.forEach(page => {
                if (page === '...') {
                    pageNumbers.innerHTML += `<span class="page-ellipsis">...</span>`;
                } else {
                    pageNumbers.innerHTML += `
                    <button class="page-btn ${page === current ? 'active' : ''}"
                            onclick="goToPage(${page})">${page}</button>
                `;
                }
            });

            // Update button states
            document.getElementById('firstPage').disabled = current === 1;
            document.getElementById('prevPage').disabled = current === 1;
            document.getElementById('nextPage').disabled = current === total;
            document.getElementById('lastPage').disabled = current === total;
        }

        function updatePageInfo(start, end, total) {
            document.getElementById('pageInfo').textContent =
                `Showing ${start}-${end} of ${total} cases`;
        }

        // Event listeners
        document.getElementById('rowsPerPage').addEventListener('change', (e) => {
            itemsPerPage = parseInt(e.target.value);
            currentPage = 1;
            displayPage(currentPage);
        });

        document.getElementById('firstPage').addEventListener('click', () => {
            if (currentPage !== 1) displayPage(1);
        });

        document.getElementById('prevPage').addEventListener('click', () => {
            if (currentPage > 1) displayPage(currentPage - 1);
        });

        document.getElementById('nextPage').addEventListener('click', () => {
            if (currentPage < totalPages) displayPage(currentPage + 1);
        });

        document.getElementById('lastPage').addEventListener('click', () => {
            if (currentPage !== totalPages) displayPage(totalPages);
        });

        // Initial display
        displayPage(1);
    }
    function animateValue(element, start, end, duration) {
        let startTimestamp = null;
        const step = (timestamp) => {
            if (!startTimestamp) startTimestamp = timestamp;
            const progress = Math.min((timestamp - startTimestamp) / duration, 1);
            const currentValue = Math.floor(progress * (end - start) + start);
            element.textContent = currentValue.toLocaleString();
            if (progress < 1) {
                window.requestAnimationFrame(step);
            }
        };
        window.requestAnimationFrame(step);
    }
    function updateAUXTimer(hours, minutes, seconds) {
        // Update ring progress
        const hoursProgress = (hours % 12) / 12 * 100;
        const minutesProgress = minutes / 60 * 100;
        const secondsProgress = seconds / 60 * 100;

        // Update rings
        updateRing('hours', hoursProgress, hours.toString().padStart(2, '0'));
        updateRing('minutes', minutesProgress, minutes.toString().padStart(2, '0'));
        updateRing('seconds', secondsProgress, seconds.toString().padStart(2, '0'));
    }

    function updateRing(unit, percentage, value) {
        const ring = document.querySelector(`.timer-ring.${unit} .timer-ring-progress`);
        const valueDisplay = document.querySelector(`.timer-ring.${unit} .timer-value`);

        const radius = ring.r.baseVal.value;
        const circumference = radius * 2 * Math.PI;
        const offset = circumference - (percentage / 100) * circumference;

        ring.style.strokeDasharray = `${circumference} ${circumference}`;
        ring.style.strokeDashoffset = offset;
        valueDisplay.textContent = value;
    }

    function updateAUXStatus(status) {
        const auxStatus = document.querySelector('.aux-status');
        const statusText = document.querySelector('.aux-status-text');

        auxStatus.dataset.status = status.toLowerCase();
        statusText.textContent = status;
    }
    function updateSummaryProgress(productive, nonProductive, offline) {
        const total = productive + nonProductive + offline;
        if (total === 0) return;

        document.querySelector('.progress.productive').style.width =
            `${(productive/total) * 100}%`;
        document.querySelector('.progress.non-productive').style.width =
            `${(nonProductive/total) * 100}%`;
        document.querySelector('.progress.offline').style.width =
            `${(offline/total) * 100}%`;
    }

    function init() {
        const styleEl = document.createElement('style');
        styleEl.innerHTML = `
    ${STYLES}
    ${CASE_MANAGEMENT_STYLES}
    .dashboard-btn {
        position: fixed;
        top: 50%;
    transform: translateY(-50%);
        right: 20px;
        z-index: 9999;
        background: #002d5b;
        color: white;
        padding: 8px 16px;
        border: none;
        border-radius: 20px;
        cursor: pointer;
        font-family: Arial, sans-serif;
        font-size: 13px;
        box-shadow: 0 2px 5px rgba(0,0,0,0.2);
        transition: all 0.3s ease;
        display: flex;
        align-items: center;
        gap: 6px;
    }

    .dashboard-btn:hover {
        background: #004280;
        transform: translateY(-2px);
        box-shadow: 0 4px 8px rgba(0,0,0,0.2);
    }

    .dashboard-btn-icon {
        width: 16px;
        height: 16px;
        fill: currentColor;
    }

    .dashboard-btn-tooltip {
        position: absolute;
        bottom: 100%;
        left: 50%;
        transform: translateX(-50%);
        background: rgba(0,0,0,0.8);
        color: white;
        padding: 4px 8px;
        border-radius: 4px;
        font-size: 11px;
        white-space: nowrap;
        opacity: 0;
        transition: opacity 0.2s;
        pointer-events: none;
        margin-bottom: 8px;
    }

    .dashboard-btn:hover .dashboard-btn-tooltip {
        opacity: 1;
    }
`;
        document.head.appendChild(styleEl);

        CaseSystem.init();
        CaseSystem.initCrossTabSync();

        if (location.hostname.includes('development') || true) { // Remove "|| true" in production
            initDebugLogging();
        }

        // Create floating dashboard button
        const button = document.createElement('button');
        button.className = 'dashboard-btn';
        button.innerHTML = `
       <svg class="dashboard-btn-icon" viewBox="0 0 24 24">
        <path d="M3 13h8V3H3v10zm0 8h8v-6H3v6zm10 0h8V11h-8v10zm0-18v6h8V3h-8z"/>
    </svg>
            `;
        button.onclick = () => {
            try {
                if (!window.dashboardWindow || window.dashboardWindow.closed) {
                    openDashboard();
                } else {
                    window.dashboardWindow.focus();
                }
            } catch (error) {
                console.error('Error opening dashboard:', error);
            }
        };
        document.body.appendChild(button);

        if (UserSystem.isLoggedIn()) {
            setInterval(() => CaseSystem.scanAllOpenTabs(), 2000);
        }
        createFloatingWidget();
    }


    function showShortcutNotification(message) {
        // Rate limiting for shortcut notifications
        const now = Date.now();
        if (this.lastShortcutNotificationTime && (now - this.lastShortcutNotificationTime) < 1000) {
            return;
        }
        this.lastShortcutNotificationTime = now;

        // Remove existing notifications
        const existingNotifications = document.querySelectorAll('.dashboard-notification');
        existingNotifications.forEach(notification => notification.remove());

        const notification = document.createElement('div');
        notification.className = 'dashboard-notification';
        notification.textContent = message;

        // Add styles if not already present
        if (!document.querySelector('#shortcut-notification-styles')) {
            const styleEl = document.createElement('style');
            styleEl.id = 'shortcut-notification-styles';
            styleEl.textContent = `
        .dashboard-notification {
            position: fixed;
            top: 20px;
            left: 50%;
            transform: translateX(-50%);
            background: #002d5b;
            color: white;
            padding: 8px 16px;
            border-radius: 4px;
            z-index: 10000;
            font-size: 14px;
            box-shadow: 0 2px 8px rgba(0,0,0,0.2);
            opacity: 0;
            transition: opacity 0.3s ease;
        }

        .dashboard-notification.visible {
            opacity: 1;
        }
    `;
            document.head.appendChild(styleEl);
        }

        document.body.appendChild(notification);

        // Trigger reflow before adding visible class
        notification.offsetHeight;

        // Show notification
        requestAnimationFrame(() => {
            notification.classList.add('visible');
        });

        // Remove after delay
        setTimeout(() => {
            notification.classList.remove('visible');
            setTimeout(() => {
                if (notification && notification.parentElement) {
                    notification.remove();
                }
            }, 300); // Wait for fade out
        }, 5000);
    }


    function initDebugLogging() {
        setInterval(() => {
            console.log('AUX Debug State:', {
                currentStatus: CaseSystem.auxState.currentStatus,
                duration: CaseSystem.auxState.duration,
                dailyTotals: CaseSystem.auxTotals.dailyTotals,
                lastStatus: CaseSystem.auxTotals.lastStatus,
                lastStatusTime: CaseSystem.auxTotals.lastStatusTime
            });
        }, 5000);
    }

    function createFloatingWidget() {
        // Check if widget already exists
        if (document.getElementById('productivity-widget')) return;

        const widget = document.createElement('div');
        widget.id = 'productivity-widget';
        widget.style.cssText = `
    position: fixed;
    right: 20px;          /* Anchored to the right */
    top: 140px;           /* Positioned below the top header */
    background: linear-gradient(135deg, #6c5ce7 0%, #a29bfe 100%); /* Adjusted to match image gradient */
    color: white;
    padding: 15px 20px;
    border-radius: 12px;
    box-shadow: 0 10px 25px rgba(0,0,0,0.2);
    z-index: 9999;
    font-family: 'Segoe UI', Tahoma, Geneva, Verdana, sans-serif;
    font-size: 13px;
    min-width: 180px;
    cursor: move;
    user-select: none;
`;


        widget.innerHTML = `
        <div style="font-weight: bold; font-size: 14px; margin-bottom: 10px; border-bottom: 1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.3); padding-bottom: 8px;">
            📊 Today's Metrics
        </div>
        <div id="widget-cases" style="margin: 5px 0;">
            <span style="opacity: 0.8;">Cases:</span> <span style="font-weight: bold; font-size: 16px;">--</span>
        </div>
        <div id="widget-aht" style="margin: 5px 0;">
            <span style="opacity: 0.8;">AHT:</span> <span style="font-weight: bold; font-size: 16px;">--</span>
        </div>
        <div id="widget-efficiency" style="margin: 5px 0;">
            <span style="opacity: 0.8;">Efficiency:</span> <span style="font-weight: bold; font-size: 16px;">--</span>
        </div>
        <div id="widget-productive" style="margin: 5px 0; font-size: 11px; opacity: 0.9; margin-top: 8px; padding-top: 8px; border-top: 1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.2);">
            <span style="opacity: 0.8;">Productive:</span> <span style="font-weight: bold;">--</span>
        </div>
    `;

        document.body.appendChild(widget);

        // Make widget draggable
        makeDraggable(widget);

        // Update widget data
        updateWidgetData();

        // Refresh every 5 seconds
        setInterval(updateWidgetData, 5000);
    }

    function updateWidgetData() {
        const casesElement = document.getElementById('widget-cases');
        const ahtElement = document.getElementById('widget-aht');
        const efficiencyElement = document.getElementById('widget-efficiency');
        const productiveElement = document.getElementById('widget-productive');

        if (!casesElement) return;

        try {
            const cases = CaseSystem.cases;
            const today = new Date();
            today.setHours(0, 0, 0, 0);

            const TRANSFER_AHT = 1.5;

            const metrics = {
                today: { paragon: 0, photon: 0, transfers: 0 },
                todayAHT: { paragon: 0, photon: 0, transfers: 0 },
                asinAdjustments: { today: 0 }
            };

            // Calculate metrics using SAME logic as dashboard
            Object.values(cases).forEach(caseData => {
                const caseDate = new Date(caseData.date);
                caseDate.setHours(0, 0, 0, 0);
                const isToday = caseDate.getTime() === today.getTime();

                if (!isToday) return;

                let type;
                let aht;

                if (caseData.isTransfer || caseData.type === 'Transfer') {
                    type = 'transfers';
                    aht = TRANSFER_AHT;
                } else {
                    type = caseData.type.toLowerCase();
                    aht = parseFloat(caseData.aht) || 0;
                }

                metrics.today[type]++;
                metrics.todayAHT[type] += aht;

                // ASIN adjustments
                if (caseData.asinCount > 3 && !caseData.isTransfer) {
                    const asinAdjustment = ((caseData.asinCount - 3) * 30) / 60;
                    metrics.asinAdjustments.today += asinAdjustment;
                }
            });

            // Calculate total AHT (SAME as dashboard)
            const todayTotalAHT = metrics.todayAHT.paragon +
                  metrics.todayAHT.photon +
                  metrics.todayAHT.transfers +
                  metrics.asinAdjustments.today;

            // Calculate total cases
            const totalCases = metrics.today.paragon + metrics.today.photon + metrics.today.transfers;

            // Get productive time (SAME as dashboard)
            const totalProductiveSeconds = CaseSystem.auxTotals.dailyTotals.productive +
                  (CaseSystem.getAuxCategory(CaseSystem.auxTotals.lastStatus) === 'productive' ?
                   CaseSystem.auxTotals.productive : 0);

            const productiveTimeInMinutes = Math.max(Math.floor(totalProductiveSeconds / 60), 1);

            // Calculate efficiency (SAME formula as dashboard)
            const efficiency = CaseSystem.calculateEfficiency(todayTotalAHT, productiveTimeInMinutes);

            // Format productive time
            const hours = Math.floor(totalProductiveSeconds / 3600);
            const minutes = Math.floor((totalProductiveSeconds % 3600) / 60);

            // Update display
            casesElement.querySelector('span:last-child').textContent = totalCases;
            ahtElement.querySelector('span:last-child').textContent = `${todayTotalAHT.toFixed(1)}m`;

            const effSpan = efficiencyElement.querySelector('span:last-child');
            effSpan.textContent = `${efficiency.toFixed(1)}%`;
            effSpan.style.color = efficiency > 100 ? '#4ade80' : '#fbbf24';

            productiveElement.querySelector('span:last-child').textContent = `${hours}h ${minutes}m`;

        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Widget update error:', error);
        }
    }

    function makeDraggable(element) {
        let pos1 = 0, pos2 = 0, pos3 = 0, pos4 = 0;

        element.onmousedown = dragMouseDown;

        function dragMouseDown(e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            pos3 = e.clientX;
            pos4 = e.clientY;
            document.onmouseup = closeDragElement;
            document.onmousemove = elementDrag;
        }

        function elementDrag(e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            pos1 = pos3 - e.clientX;
            pos2 = pos4 - e.clientY;
            pos3 = e.clientX;
            pos4 = e.clientY;
            element.style.top = (element.offsetTop - pos2) + "px";
            element.style.left = (element.offsetLeft - pos1) + "px";
            element.style.transform = 'none'; // Remove centering transform when dragging
        }

        function closeDragElement() {
            document.onmouseup = null;
            document.onmousemove = null;
        }
    }


    init();
})();
